##### **User-Aware Active Knowledge Acquisition for Emotional Support Dialogue**
2605.29715v1 by Mufan Xu, Kehai Chen, Jiahao Hu, Xinchao Xu, Muyun Yang, Tiejun Zhao, Min Zhang

Emotional support plays an important role in dialogue systems, and its success depends on adapting to a user's evolving and implicit needs across multi-turn interactions while leveraging the strong reasoning capacity of large language models. However, since signals about user needs are often weak, indirect, and can only be disambiguated through multi-turn interaction, existing emotional support methods often struggle to acquire and generalize relevant conversational knowledge efficiently. To bridge this gap, we introduce User-Aware Active Knowledge Acquisition (UKA), a gradient-free active dialogue learning framework that explicitly represents uncertainty about user needs and incorporates active learning into both knowledge acquisition and response selection.We propose a Theory-of-Mind uncertainty estimation mechanism that allows the model to prioritize responses, thereby eliciting more informative user feedback. UKA is capable of efficiently exploring user-aligned conversational knowledge during training while maintaining robustness at test time. Experiments across multiple dialogue benchmarks and model architectures demonstrate that our approach consistently outperforms strong baselines in dialogue quality and user alignment.

摘要：情感支持在對話系統中扮演著重要角色，其成功依賴於適應用戶在多輪互動中不斷演變的隱性需求，同時利用大型語言模型的強大推理能力。<lb/>然而，由於用戶需求的信號往往是微弱的、間接的，且只能通過多輪互動來消歧，因此現有的情感支持方法常常難以有效獲取和概括相關的對話知識。<lb/>為了彌補這一差距，我們提出了用戶感知主動知識獲取（UKA），這是一個無梯度的主動對話學習框架，明確表示對用戶需求的不確定性，並將主動學習納入知識獲取和回應選擇中。<lb/>我們提出了一種心智理論不確定性估計機制，使模型能夠優先考慮回應，從而引出更具信息量的用戶反饋。<lb/>UKA 能夠在訓練過程中有效探索與用戶對齊的對話知識，同時在測試時保持穩健性。<lb/>在多個對話基準和模型架構上的實驗表明，我們的方法在對話質量和用戶對齊方面始終超越強基線。

##### **Beyond Trajectory Rewards: Step-level Credit Assignment for Agentic Search via Graph Modeling**
2605.29697v1 by Yuchen Liu, Yingjie Feng, Lixiong Qin, Jiasi Chen, Jianing Yu, Sheng Gao, Sheng Yang, Weiran Xu

In Agentic Search, trajectory-level outcome rewards fail to quantify the behavioral contributions of individual steps, while existing step-level reward methods typically rely on costly tree sampling. We view world knowledge as a latent world graph and each IS task as search within a latent task graph, where effective steps should make graph progress toward the answer node. Based on this prior, we propose Graph-Distance Contribution Reward (GDCR), a step-level process reward that scores newly-retrieved and newly-cited entities by their distance to the answer node in a training-time Entity-Relation (ER) graph. We further propose Step Advantage Policy Optimization (SAPO), which converts GDCR into step-level advantages and combines them with trajectory-level outcome advantages. Experiments on four challenging benchmarks validate the effectiveness of our method.

摘要：在代理搜索中，軌跡級的結果獎勵無法量化單個步驟的行為貢獻，而現有的步驟級獎勵方法通常依賴於昂貴的樹採樣。我們將世界知識視為潛在的世界圖，並將每個IS任務視為在潛在的任務圖中進行搜索，其中有效的步驟應該使圖向答案節點進展。基於這一前提，我們提出了圖距貢獻獎勵（GDCR），這是一種步驟級過程獎勵，通過它們與答案節點在訓練時的實體-關係（ER）圖中的距離來對新檢索和新引用的實體進行評分。我們進一步提出了步驟優勢策略優化（SAPO），將GDCR轉換為步驟級優勢，並將其與軌跡級結果優勢相結合。在四個具有挑戰性的基準上的實驗驗證了我們方法的有效性。

##### **GRASP: Gated Regression-Aware Skill Proposer for Self-Improving LLM Agents**
2605.29668v1 by Johannes Moll, Jean-Philippe Corbeil, Jiazhen Pan, Martin Hadamitzky, Daniel Rueckert, Lisa Adams, Keno Bressem

LLM agents acting in structured environments fail in operational rather than conversational ways, and reliability depends on procedural knowledge of the environment. Prior self-improvement methods accumulate natural-language guidance without checking that each new item preserves previously correct behavior, so a note that fixes one trajectory can silently regress another. We introduce GRASP (Gated Regression-Aware Skill Proposer), which treats agent improvement as a sequence of edits to a bounded skill library, admitting each candidate only if it produces a net improvement on a balanced held-out probe under a hard regression budget. We evaluate GRASP across five base models (gpt-oss-120b, DeepSeek V4 Flash, Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite, GPT-4.1, GPT-5.4) on two FHIR-based clinical benchmarks. On MedAgentBench, GRASP lifts gpt-oss-120b from 40.6% to 88.8%, exceeds the strongest of five self-improvement baselines by 21.0 points, and improves every other base model by 17.2 to 40.3 points. Ablations attribute the gain to comparative proposal generation, the acceptance gate, and the hard regression budget rather than to skill writing itself, which without validation is no better than using no skills. The mechanism generalizes beyond the clinical domain, improving agents on three of four non-clinical environments and remaining flat only where the action space is open-ended. Frozen libraries transfer across models, where skills from a stronger model improve weaker executors beyond what they learn for themselves while the reverse does not, an asymmetry that no ungated baseline reproduces.

摘要：LLM 代理在結構化環境中運作時，失敗的原因是操作性而非對話性，可靠性取決於對環境的程序性知識。先前的自我改進方法累積自然語言指導，但未檢查每個新項目是否保持之前正確的行為，因此修正一個軌跡的註解可能會默默地使另一個軌跡退步。我們引入 GRASP（Gated Regression-Aware Skill Proposer），將代理的改進視為對有限技能庫的一系列編輯，僅在候選者在硬性回歸預算下對平衡的保留探針產生淨改善時才接受。我們在兩個基於 FHIR 的臨床基準上評估 GRASP，涵蓋五個基模型（gpt-oss-120b、DeepSeek V4 Flash、Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite、GPT-4.1、GPT-5.4）。在 MedAgentBench 上，GRASP 將 gpt-oss-120b 的表現從 40.6% 提升至 88.8%，超過五個自我改進基線中最強的模型 21.0 分，並使其他每個基模型提高 17.2 到 40.3 分。消融實驗將增益歸因於比較提案生成、接受閘和硬性回歸預算，而非技能編寫本身，因為在沒有驗證的情況下，這樣做並不比不使用技能更好。該機制在臨床領域之外也具有通用性，改善了四個非臨床環境中的三個代理，只有在行動空間無限制的情況下保持平穩。凍結的庫可以跨模型轉移，強模型的技能使弱執行者的表現超過他們自己學到的，而反之則不然，這種不對稱性是任何未經閘控的基線所無法重現的。

##### **LLM-Evolved Domain-Independent Heuristics for Symbolic AI Planning**
2605.29649v1 by Elliot Gestrin, Jendrik Seipp

Heuristic search is the dominant paradigm in symbolic AI planning, and the strongest heuristics are the result of decades of work by planning researchers. Recent work has shown that large language models (LLMs) can design heuristics for individual planning domains, but no LLM-generated heuristic has so far worked on arbitrary planning tasks. In this paper, we use evolutionary search to produce the first LLM-generated domain-independent heuristics that exceed the hand-engineered state of the art. We let an LLM mutate parent heuristics written in C++, store candidates in a MAP-Elites archive keyed on informedness and speed and calculate fitness scores by blending coverage with solving time. To place the evolved programs in context, we additionally benchmark a broad set of hand-engineered heuristics on their informedness-speed tradeoff, which to our knowledge has not been done before. On unseen testing domains, our best evolved heuristic solves more tasks than even the strongest baseline, with our full heuristic suite spanning the Pareto frontier of said tradeoff. We also find that seeding evolution from the trivial blind heuristic outperforms seeding from the strong FF heuristic, even when the resulting program is itself an FF variant, and that LLM reasoning effort affects how often candidates compile much more than the quality of those that do. Because the evolved programs are plain C++, they slot into existing planners as drop-in replacements and inherit the soundness and completeness guarantees of the underlying search.

摘要：啟發式搜尋是符號人工智慧規劃中的主導範式，而最強的啟發式方法是規劃研究人員經過數十年努力的結果。最近的研究顯示，大型語言模型（LLMs）可以為個別規劃領域設計啟發式方法，但到目前為止，尚未有LLM生成的啟發式方法能在任意規劃任務上運作。在本文中，我們使用進化搜尋來產生第一個超越手工設計的最先進水平的LLM生成的領域獨立啟發式方法。我們讓LLM變異用C++編寫的父啟發式，將候選者存儲在以知識性和速度為鍵的MAP-Elites檔案中，並通過將覆蓋率與解決時間混合來計算適應度分數。為了將進化的程序放在上下文中，我們還基準測試了一組廣泛的手工設計啟發式方法，評估其知識性與速度的權衡，據我們所知，這在之前並未進行過。在未見過的測試領域中，我們最佳的進化啟發式方法解決的任務數量超過了最強基準，即使我們的完整啟發式套件也跨越了上述權衡的Pareto邊界。我們還發現，從平凡的盲啟發式開始進化的效果優於從強大的FF啟發式開始，即使最終的程序本身是FF變體，並且LLM推理的努力影響候選者的編譯頻率，遠超過那些能夠編譯的質量。由於進化的程序是純C++，它們可以作為即插即用的替代品融入現有的規劃器，並繼承底層搜尋的健全性和完整性保證。

##### **Verifiable Rewards Beyond Math and Code: Lightweight Corpus-Grounded Process Supervision for Factual Question Answering**
2605.29648v1 by Shicheng Fan, Haochang Hao, Dehai Min, Weihao Liu, Philip S. Yu, Lu Cheng

Applying reinforcement learning to improve factual accuracy in knowledge-intensive question answering faces a reward design dilemma. Response-level rewards provide only coarse supervision and cannot distinguish correct from incorrect statements within a reasoning trace. Sentence-level alternatives offer finer-grained feedback, but typically rely on NLI verifiers, LLM judges, or knowledge-verification pipelines that are expensive to deploy at RL scale and often unreliable for rare-entity facts, where accurate reward signals are especially important. We propose CorVer (Corpus Verify), a lightweight, plug-in-ready process reward that replaces neural verifiers with a corpus-grounded signal derived from Wikipedia co-occurrence statistics. CorVer assigns sentence-level credit and maps it to token-level advantages via a simple alignment, requiring only a 0.5B extractor and a single corpus lookup per sentence. Across 30 (model, benchmark) cells spanning six instruction-tuned models (3B to 14B) and five QA benchmarks, CorVer improves over the raw baseline for every cell, with an average TriviaQA gain of +4.1 pp. It also outperforms four neural-verifier baselines in 18 of 20 cells under their feasible configurations, while training 4.8 to 8.4x faster.

摘要：應用增強學習來提高知識密集型問題回答中的事實準確性面臨獎勵設計的困境。回應級別的獎勵僅提供粗略的監督，無法在推理過程中區分正確與不正確的陳述。句子級別的替代方案提供了更細緻的反饋，但通常依賴於NLI驗證器、LLM評判或知識驗證管道，這些在增強學習規模下部署成本高昂，且對於稀有實體事實往往不可靠，而準確的獎勵信號在這些情況下尤其重要。我們提出了CorVer（Corpus Verify），這是一種輕量級的即插即用過程獎勵，通過來自維基百科共現統計的語料庫基礎信號取代神經驗證器。CorVer為句子級別分配信用，並通過簡單的對齊將其映射到令牌級別的優勢，只需每句話0.5B的提取器和一次語料庫查詢。在涵蓋六個指令調整模型（3B到14B）和五個QA基準的30個（模型，基準）單元中，CorVer在每個單元上都超越了原始基線，平均TriviaQA增益為+4.1個百分點。它在20個單元中的18個單元下也超越了四個神經驗證器基線，並且訓練速度快了4.8到8.4倍。

##### **Classification of non-analyzable word types in web documents to implement an effective Korean e-learning system**
2605.29638v1 by Sang-Taek Park, Ae-Lim Ahn, Eric Laporte, Jee-Sun Nam

E-learning systems should deliver contents that reflect various phenomena of the language as it is used. In addition to formal Korean, e-learning systems that would include real-world Korean expressions such as those in web documents, mobile text messages, or twitter posts, would be useful to high-level learners. We construct two types of corpora: one is made of formal documents like online news articles; the other is made of informal documents like customer reviews about new products in web blogs. By comparing these corpora, we show how expressions differ in these two types of corpora. We survey the main characteristics of the informal corpus. Given that a significant proportion of text is informal, we propose Local Grammar Graphs (LGG) as an appropriate model to treat them effectively in Korean e-learning systems.

摘要：E-learning 系統應該提供反映語言使用中各種現象的內容。除了正式的韓語外，包含網頁文件、手機簡訊或推特帖子的現實韓語表達的電子學習系統，對於高級學習者將會非常有用。我們構建了兩種類型的語料庫：一種是由正式文件組成，如線上新聞文章；另一種是由非正式文件組成，如網誌中關於新產品的顧客評論。通過比較這些語料庫，我們展示了這兩種類型的語料庫中表達的差異。我們調查了非正式語料庫的主要特徵。考慮到相當一部分文本是非正式的，我們提出了局部語法圖（LGG）作為在韓語電子學習系統中有效處理它們的合適模型。

##### **Evaluating Cross-lingual Knowledge Consistency in Code-Mixed vis-a-vis Indian Languages using IndicKLAR**
2605.29637v1 by Debajyoti Mazumder, Divyansh Pathak, Prashant Kodali, Aditya Joshi, Akshay Agarwal, Jasabanta Patro

Large language models recall knowledge reliably in English but often fail on the same query posed in a lower-resourced language -- a crosslingual consistency gap that remains underexplored for Indian languages and their code-mixed counterparts. To study this gap, we introduce IndiKLAR, an Indic extension of the KLAR-CLC benchmark covering 18 of the 22 scheduled Indian languages and pairing them with code-mixed variants for 11 widely used language pairs, with native-speaker verification of both monolingual and code-mixed variants for these 11 settings. This three-way alignment offers a unique opportunity to examine how knowledge recall consistency varies across the spectrum of English, code-mixed, and native Indian language inputs. Evaluating across nine open-weight models, we find that the native-language accuracy gap to English can reach $\sim$0.50, while code-mixed inputs close most of it -- bringing performance within $\sim$0.05 of English without any model-level intervention. Motivated by this, we evaluate several prompting strategies that vary in how language conversion is exposed, including a two-stage translate-then-answer setup, a one-stage joint translation-and-answer prompt, and Translate-in-Thought (TinT) -- a single-step strategy in which the model converts the input internally and emits only the final answer. Across the performance trajectory native $\rightarrow$ code-mixed $\rightarrow$ English, we identify a consistent flip point -- the boundary between incorrect and correct prediction -- that lies between the native and code-mixed settings. Interestingly, this holds whether the trajectory is induced by the input surface form or by the model's internal conversion process.

摘要：大型語言模型在英語中可靠地回憶知識，但在低資源語言中對同一查詢的表現往往不佳——這是一個在印度語言及其混合代碼對應語言中仍未充分探索的跨語言一致性差距。為了研究這一差距，我們引入了IndiKLAR，這是一個KLAR-CLC基準的印度擴展，涵蓋22種計劃中的印度語言中的18種，並為11對廣泛使用的語言配對混合代碼變體，並對這11個設置中的單語和混合代碼變體進行母語者驗證。這種三方對齊提供了一個獨特的機會來檢查知識回憶一致性在英語、混合代碼和本土印度語言輸入之間的變化。在九個開放權重模型的評估中，我們發現母語到英語的準確性差距可以達到約0.50，而混合代碼輸入則縮小了大部分差距——使性能在沒有任何模型級別干預的情況下接近英語約0.05。受到此啟發，我們評估了幾種提示策略，這些策略在語言轉換的曝光方式上有所不同，包括兩階段的翻譯後回答設置、一階段的聯合翻譯和回答提示，以及翻譯思維（TinT）——一種單步策略，其中模型在內部轉換輸入並僅發出最終答案。在母語 $\rightarrow$ 混合代碼 $\rightarrow$ 英語的性能軌跡中，我們識別出一個一致的翻轉點——錯誤預測和正確預測之間的邊界——位於母語和混合代碼設置之間。有趣的是，這一點無論是由輸入表面形式還是模型的內部轉換過程引起的，都成立。

##### **Predicting Causal Effects from Natural Language Queries using Structured Representations**
2605.29631v1 by Giuliano Martinelli, Piriyakorn Piriyatamwong, Abelardo Carlos Martinez Lorenzo, Jasmin Baier, Riccardo Orlando, Satvik Garg, Sharif Kazemi, Linxi Wang, Arianna Legovini, Samuel Fraiberger

Randomized controlled trials are a cornerstone of medicine and the social sciences as they enable reliable estimates of causal effects. However, they are costly and time-consuming to conduct, motivating interest in predicting causal effects from existing experimental evidence. Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance on knowledge-intensive tasks, raising the question of whether these models can be used for forecasting causal effect sizes. To investigate this, we introduce Query2Effect, a new large-scale benchmark consisting of more than 72,000 natural language questions aligned with experiment descriptions, created to simulate realistic information-seeking scenarios by varying query specificity along dimensions of implicitness, abstraction, and ambiguity. We then propose a two-step framework that first generates a synthetic structured representation of a query before predicting effect size using a supervised encoder model. Experiments show that finetuning plays a crucial role in improving prediction performance, with absolute error reducing by -27% up to -71% compared to prompted out-of-the-box LLMs, and that our two-step framework is beneficial for out-of-domain generalization, highlighting the benefits of separating semantic interpretation from numerical effect estimation.

摘要：隨機對照試驗是醫學和社會科學的基石，因為它們能夠提供可靠的因果效應估計。然而，這些試驗的進行成本高且耗時，這促使人們對從現有實驗證據中預測因果效應產生興趣。最近在大型語言模型（LLMs）方面的進展顯示出在知識密集型任務上表現出色，這引發了這些模型是否可以用於預測因果效應大小的問題。為了調查這一點，我們引入了Query2Effect，一個新的大規模基準，包含超過72,000個與實驗描述對齊的自然語言問題，旨在通過在隱含性、抽象性和模糊性等維度上變化查詢的具體性來模擬現實的信息尋求場景。然後，我們提出了一個兩步框架，首先生成查詢的合成結構化表示，然後使用監督編碼模型預測效應大小。實驗顯示，微調在提高預測性能方面起著至關重要的作用，與直接使用未經調整的LLMs相比，絕對誤差減少了27%至71%，而且我們的兩步框架對於域外泛化是有益的，突顯了將語義解釋與數值效應估計分開的好處。

##### **CONCAT: Consensus- and Confidence-Driven Ad Hoc Teaming for Efficient LLM-Based Multi-Agent Systems**
2605.29612v1 by Ziyang Ma, Dingyi Zhang, Sichu Liang, Jiajia Chu, Pengfei Xia, Hui Zang, Deyu Zhou

Although large language model (LLM) based multi-agent systems (MAS) show their capability to solve complex tasks and achieve higher performance over single agent systems, they lead to huge computational overheads because of heavy communication between agents. Previous research has made efforts to train a sparse multi-agent graph or fine-tune a planner to orchestrate the workflow better. However, such extra training processes introduce computational costs and limit MAS to specific domains, therefore compromising their generalizability. In this paper, we propose CONCAT, a training-free multi-agent collaboration framework based on CONsensus and Confidence-driven Ad hoc Teaming to efficiently organize agent interactions. Specifically, agents are clustered based on their initial answers, and leaders of each cluster are selected based on the agents' confidence. Then, a heuristic function based on the Theory of Mind is designed to predict the collaboration benefits between every two leaders according to their answers and confidence. Finally, an ad hoc multi-agent network is organized after evicting a percentage of communications based on the predicted benefits. Experiments across three LLMs and three benchmarks show that CONCAT achieves up to 2.02x higher efficiency (accuracy/latency ratio) than LLM-Debate and outperforms training-aware methods such as AgentDropout, while reducing average latency by 50.1% on Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct, without any task-specific training.

摘要：儘管基於大型語言模型 (LLM) 的多代理系統 (MAS) 展現了解決複雜任務的能力並在性能上超越單一代理系統，但由於代理之間的重通信，它們導致了巨大的計算開銷。以往的研究已經努力訓練稀疏的多代理圖或微調計劃者，以更好地協調工作流程。然而，這些額外的訓練過程引入了計算成本，並將 MAS 限制在特定領域，從而妨礙了它們的通用性。在本文中，我們提出了 CONCAT，一個基於共識和信心驅動的臨時團隊的無需訓練的多代理協作框架，以有效組織代理互動。具體而言，代理根據其初始答案進行聚類，並根據代理的信心選擇每個聚類的領導者。然後，根據他們的答案和信心，設計一個基於心智理論的啟發式函數來預測每兩位領導者之間的協作收益。最後，在根據預測的收益驅逐一定比例的通信後，組織了一個臨時多代理網絡。在三個 LLM 和三個基準測試中的實驗顯示，CONCAT 的效率（準確性/延遲比）比 LLM-Debate 高出最多 2.02 倍，並且在 Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct 上的平均延遲降低了 50.1%，而無需任何特定任務的訓練。

##### **Learning Context-Conditioned Predicate Semantics via Prototype Feedback**
2605.29610v1 by NamGyu Jung, Chang Choi

In scene graph generation, a central challenge is modeling polysemous predicates whose meanings shift across contexts. Prior approaches address this issue by decomposing predicates into multiple static prototypes or retrieving semantically similar exemplars. However, these strategies keep predicate representations static and cannot reorganize semantics to reflect image-specific evidence, leading to systematic confusions in ambiguous contexts. We propose AlignG, which learns context-conditioned predicate semantics via prototype feedback. AlignG infers context-conditioned predicate semantics from the relation candidates within each image and feeds the adapted semantics back to recalibrate relation representations. The learning objective anchors this adaptation to global semantic centers, preventing semantic drift while still allowing selective reorganization when the scene provides consistent relational cues. Experiments on VG-150 and GQA-200 show consistent improvements over state-of-the-art baselines, with F@100 improvements of +1.4 on VG-150 and +2.7 on GQA-200 under SGDet. We further visualize per-image prototype similarity shifts and observe coherent context-dependent reorganization where prototypes selectively merge or separate predicates according to scene evidence. The code is available at https://github.com/Namgyu97/AlignG-SGG.pytorch.

摘要：在場景圖生成中，一個主要挑戰是建模多義謂詞，其意義在不同上下文中會有所變化。先前的方法通過將謂詞分解為多個靜態原型或檢索語義相似的例子來解決這個問題。然後，這些策略保持謂詞表示的靜態性，無法重新組織語義以反映特定於圖像的證據，導致在模糊上下文中出現系統性的混淆。我們提出了AlignG，通過原型反饋學習上下文條件的謂詞語義。AlignG從每個圖像中的關係候選者推斷上下文條件的謂詞語義，並將調整後的語義反饋以重新校準關係表示。學習目標將這種調整固定在全球語義中心，防止語義漂移，同時在場景提供一致的關係線索時仍允許選擇性重新組織。在VG-150和GQA-200上的實驗顯示出相對於最先進基準的一致性改進，在SGDet下，VG-150的F@100改進了+1.4，GQA-200則改進了+2.7。我們進一步可視化每個圖像的原型相似性變化，觀察到一致的上下文依賴重新組織，原型根據場景證據選擇性地合併或分離謂詞。該代碼可在 https://github.com/Namgyu97/AlignG-SGG.pytorch 獲得。

##### **GAPD: Gold-Action Policy Distillation for Agentic Reinforcement Learning in Knowledge Base Question Answering**
2605.29584v1 by Xin Sun, Jianan Xie, Zhongqi Chen, Qiang Liu, Shu Wu, Bowen Song, Weiqiang Wang, Zilei Wang, Liang Wang

Reinforcement learning (RL) is a natural fit for agentic knowledge base question answering (KBQA), where a model must issue executable actions, observe knowledge-base feedback, and eventually return an answer. However, current RL-based KBQA systems mainly optimize sparse rewards from the final answer, leaving intermediate action errors weakly supervised. This is especially limiting for logical-form annotated KBQA benchmarks: gold logical forms can be converted into executable action sequences, but existing pipelines use them mainly for warm-start data construction rather than for on-policy RL updates. We propose GAPD, a training-time Gold-Action Policy Distillation framework that adds dense token-level guidance to outcome-based RL. To align gold actions with on-policy student rollouts, GAPD uses MID-ANCHOR MATCHING: it treats the intermediate entities reached during student exploration and gold execution as state anchors, and matches student states to gold states through these explored entity sets. The current policy conditioned on this aligned gold action serves as a stop-gradient teacher, whose token distribution is distilled back to the ordinary student policy over generated action-token spans. GAPD consistently surpasses the current state of the art on WebQSP, GrailQA, and GraphQ.

摘要：強化學習（RL）自然適合於代理知識庫問題回答（KBQA），在這裡模型必須發出可執行的行動，觀察知識庫的反饋，並最終返回答案。<lb/>然而，目前基於RL的KBQA系統主要優化來自最終答案的稀疏獎勵，導致中間行動錯誤的監督較弱。<lb/>這對於邏輯形式註釋的KBQA基準特別有限：金標邏輯形式可以轉換為可執行的行動序列，但現有的流程主要將其用於熱啟動數據構建，而不是用於政策內的RL更新。<lb/>我們提出GAPD，一個訓練時的金行動政策蒸餾框架，為基於結果的RL添加了密集的標記級指導。<lb/>為了將金行動與政策內的學生展開對齊，GAPD使用MID-ANCHOR MATCHING：它將在學生探索和金執行過程中達到的中間實體視為狀態錨點，並通過這些探索的實體集將學生狀態與金狀態匹配。<lb/>基於這個對齊的金行動的當前政策作為停止梯度的教師，其標記分佈被蒸餾回生成的行動標記範圍內的普通學生政策。<lb/>GAPD在WebQSP、GrailQA和GraphQ上始終超越當前的最先進技術。

##### **Planning with the Views via Scene Self-Exploration**
2605.29563v1 by Kangrui Wang, Linjie Li, Zhengyuan Yang, Shiqi Chen, Zihan Wang, Li Fei-Fei, Jiajun Wu, Leonidas Guibas, Lijuan Wang, Manling Li

Can VLMs predict how each camera move changes the view, and plan many such moves ahead? We call this capability view planning, requiring (1)understanding how a single action transforms the view, and (2)composing many such transformations across multi-turn plans to identify a target view. We probe both abilities in our proposed ViewSuite, a 3D point-cloud environment on real ScanNet scenes. Across 13 frontier VLMs, a critical planning gap emerges: they possess basic view-action knowledge but fail to compose it across multi-turn plans, with the gap widening as viewpoint distance grows. To close this gap, we propose an iterative framework that alternates self-exploration with view graph distillation. The key insight is that all exploration trajectories, regardless of their outcome, collectively form a view graph that compactly captures how viewpoints connect across a scene. Distilling this graph into diverse supervised tasks reshapes the policy distribution and overcomes the sparse rewards that stall pure RL. This improves Qwen2.5-VL-7B from 2.5% to 47.8% on interactive view planning, surpassing GPT-5.4 Pro (18.5%) and Gemini 3.1 Pro (21.4%). Self-exploration emerges as a promising path toward VLMs that can actively reason and plan in 3D space.

摘要：VLM能否預測每次相機移動如何改變視角，並提前計劃多次這樣的移動？我們稱這種能力為視角規劃，這需要(1)理解單一行動如何轉變視角，以及(2)在多輪計劃中組合多次這樣的轉變以識別目標視角。我們在提出的ViewSuite中探討這兩種能力，這是一個基於真實ScanNet場景的3D點雲環境。在13個前沿VLM中，出現了一個關鍵的規劃差距：它們擁有基本的視角-行動知識，但未能在多輪計劃中組合這些知識，隨著視點距離的增長，這一差距越來越大。為了縮小這一差距，我們提出了一個迭代框架，交替進行自我探索和視圖圖的提煉。關鍵的見解是，所有探索軌跡無論其結果如何，集體形成了一個視圖圖，緊湊地捕捉了視點如何在場景中連接。將這個圖提煉成多樣的監督任務重塑了策略分佈，克服了純強化學習中停滯的稀疏獎勵。這使得Qwen2.5-VL-7B在互動視角規劃中的表現從2.5%提高到47.8%，超越了GPT-5.4 Pro（18.5%）和Gemini 3.1 Pro（21.4%）。自我探索成為通向能夠在3D空間中主動推理和規劃的VLM的有希望的途徑。

##### **ParaTool: Shifting Tool Representations from Context to Parameters**
2605.29561v1 by Zekai Yu, Qi Meng, Qizhi Chu, Yu Hao, Chuan Shi, Cheng Yang

Tool calling extends large language models (LLMs) by enabling grounded interaction with external executable interfaces, thereby supporting environment-coupled problem solving. However, mainstream in-context learning (ICL) approaches typically incorporate detailed tool documentation and usage examples directly into the context. This results in substantial inference overhead and heightened risks of hallucination as the context length grows. Conversely, while tuning-based methods improve general tool-calling capabilities, they often fail to effectively internalize the specific details of previously seen tools, thereby retaining a dependency on in-context documentation. To address these limitations, we propose ParaTool, a framework that projects each tool into a dedicated, loadable set of parameters. By equipping a dynamic integration of these parameterized tools, the LLM can perform tool calling without relying on in-context documents or examples. Specifically, our approach consists of three stages: (1) parametric tool pre-training encapsulates the knowledge of different tools into independent parameter modules; (2) soft tool selection employs a gating network to dynamically weigh and aggregate relevant tool parameters; and (3) parametric tool fine-tuning jointly updates tool parameters to align the training and inference processes. Experiments on Stable ToolBench and BFCL demonstrate that ParaTool significantly outperforms strong ICL-based baselines, achieving superior performance while reducing computational complexity.

摘要：工具調用擴展了大型語言模型（LLMs），通過啟用與外部可執行接口的基於環境的互動，從而支持環境耦合的問題解決。<lb/>然而，主流的上下文學習（ICL）方法通常將詳細的工具文檔和使用示例直接納入上下文中。<lb/>這導致了可觀的推理開銷和隨著上下文長度增長而加劇的幻覺風險。<lb/>相反，雖然基於調整的方法改善了通用的工具調用能力，但它們往往無法有效內化先前見過的工具的具體細節，從而仍然依賴於上下文文檔。<lb/>為了解決這些限制，我們提出了ParaTool，一個將每個工具投影到專用的可加載參數集的框架。<lb/>通過配備這些參數化工具的動態整合，LLM可以在不依賴上下文文檔或示例的情況下執行工具調用。<lb/>具體而言，我們的方法包括三個階段：（1）參數化工具預訓練將不同工具的知識封裝到獨立的參數模塊中；（2）軟工具選擇使用門控網絡動態加權和聚合相關的工具參數；（3）參數化工具微調共同更新工具參數，以對齊訓練和推理過程。<lb/>在Stable ToolBench和BFCL上的實驗表明，ParaTool顯著超越了強大的基於ICL的基準，實現了更優的性能，同時降低了計算複雜性。

##### **From Blind Guess to Informed Judgment: Teaching LLMs to Evaluate Materials by Building Knowledge-Augmented Preference Signals**
2605.29555v1 by Yeyong Yu, Wenya Hu, Xing Wu, Quan Qian

As candidate generation and high-throughput experimentation advance, the primary bottleneck in materials discovery is shifting from property prediction to making reliable evaluations among massive candidate sets. We propose a Knowledge-Augmented Preference Signals Framework, MaterEval, that automatically produces, for the same candidate, two evaluations: an informed judgment that follows expert rules and provides supporting evidence, and a rule-removed blind guess. By pairing the two evaluations as preference data, we guide general-purpose large language models (LLMs), originally lacking materials-specific criteria, from intuitive judgment toward reliable evaluation supported by explicit evidence. To balance throughput, cost, and reliability, we further introduce a fast-slow reasoning scheme that decouples large-scale rapid screening from in-depth review on a small subset. Using high-entropy alloy (HEA) assessment as a case study, we show that, without external retrieval and relying solely on internalized capabilities, small open-source LLMs achieve substantial gains in accuracy, conclusion consistency, and evidence discrimination, approaching the performance of rule-based closed-source LLMs. These results demonstrate that expert rules can be systematically transformed into learnable preference signals, enabling a low-cost and deployable evaluation module for autonomous materials discovery loops.

摘要：隨著候選生成和高通量實驗的進步，材料發現的主要瓶頸正在從性質預測轉向在大量候選集之間進行可靠評估。我們提出了一個知識增強偏好信號框架，MaterEval，該框架自動為同一候選產生兩個評估：一個遵循專家規則並提供支持證據的知情判斷，以及一個去除規則的盲目猜測。通過將這兩個評估配對作為偏好數據，我們引導原本缺乏材料特定標準的一般性大型語言模型（LLMs），從直觀判斷轉向由明確證據支持的可靠評估。為了平衡通量、成本和可靠性，我們進一步引入了一種快慢推理方案，將大規模快速篩選與對小子集的深入審查解耦。以高熵合金（HEA）評估為案例研究，我們顯示，無需外部檢索，僅依賴內部化能力，小型開源LLMs在準確性、結論一致性和證據區別上取得了顯著提升，接近基於規則的閉源LLMs的性能。這些結果表明，專家規則可以系統地轉化為可學習的偏好信號，從而為自主材料發現循環提供一個低成本且可部署的評估模塊。

##### **UI-KOBE: Knowledge-Oriented Behavior Exploration for Lightweight Graph-Guided GUI Agents**
2605.29534v1 by Yuxiang Chai, Han Xiao, Xinyu Fu, Jinpeng Chen, Rui Liu, Hongsheng Li

Recent advances in mobile GUI agents have shown strong potential for automating mobile tasks, but most effective systems still depend on large vision-language models for screenshot understanding and long-horizon planning. Small GUI agents that can be deployed directly on mobile devices are more attractive for practical use, offering lower inference cost and better protection of sensitive on-device information. However, due to limited model capacity, such lightweight agents remain unreliable when planning and executing GUI tasks end-to-end from screenshots alone. We propose Knowledge-Oriented Behavior Exploration (\textbf{UI-KOBE}), a framework that improves lightweight mobile GUI agents with reusable app-specific graph knowledge. UI-KOBE first autonomously explores a mobile application and constructs an app knowledge graph, where nodes represent distinct UI states and edges represent executable transitions. At runtime, a lightweight GUI agent uses the graph as external guidance: given a user task and the current screenshot, it identifies the current graph node and selects among self-loop actions, neighboring transitions, task completion, or fallback free actions associated with that node. By supporting runtime decisions with app-specific graph guidance, UI-KOBE reduces the burden of end-to-end GUI planning and helps lightweight models perform mobile GUI tasks more effectively, offering a practical step toward efficient, interpretable, and privacy-conscious on-device GUI agents.

摘要：最近在移動 GUI 代理方面的進展顯示出自動化移動任務的強大潛力，但大多數有效系統仍依賴大型視覺-語言模型進行截圖理解和長期規劃。可以直接部署在移動設備上的小型 GUI 代理對於實際使用更具吸引力，因為它們提供了較低的推理成本和更好的敏感設備信息保護。然而，由於模型容量有限，這些輕量級代理在僅依賴截圖進行端到端的 GUI 任務規劃和執行時仍然不可靠。我們提出了知識導向行為探索（\textbf{UI-KOBE}），這是一個通過可重用的應用特定圖知識來改進輕量級移動 GUI 代理的框架。UI-KOBE 首先自主探索一個移動應用並構建一個應用知識圖，其中節點代表不同的 UI 狀態，邊代表可執行的轉換。在運行時，輕量級 GUI 代理使用該圖作為外部指導：給定用戶任務和當前截圖，它識別當前圖節點並在自環動作、相鄰轉換、任務完成或與該節點相關的回退自由動作之間進行選擇。通過用應用特定的圖指導支持運行時決策，UI-KOBE 減輕了端到端 GUI 規劃的負擔，並幫助輕量級模型更有效地執行移動 GUI 任務，為高效、可解釋和注重隱私的設備內 GUI 代理邁出了實際的一步。

##### **KBF: Knowledge Boundary as Fingerprint for Language Model and Black-Box API Auditing**
2605.29524v1 by Yijia Fang, Yiqing Feng, Bingyu Li, Mingxun Zhou

Relay and reseller APIs increasingly intermediate access to large language models (LLMs), but users have no direct way to verify that a claimed endpoint is actually serving the advertised model. 2605.29522v1 by Ziyue Yang, Da Ma, Hanqi Li, Zijian Wang, Tiancheng Huang, Zijian Hu, Chenrun Wang, Yunzhe Zhang, Xiaobao Wu, Kai Yu, Lu Chen

To enhance depth, DeepSurvey extracts structured keynotes from full-text papers, models cross-paper relationships through clustering and comparative analysis, and integrates code-repository analysis to recover implementation-level details. ##### **MINDGAMES: A Live Arena for Evaluating Social and Strategic Reasoning in Multi-Agent LLMs**
2605.29512v1 by Kevin Wang, Anna Thöni, Benjamin Kempinski, Bobby Cheng, Jianzhu Yao, Benjamin Finch, Leon Guertler, Viraj Nadkarni, Yihan Jiang, Aliaksei Korshuk, Alexander Buyantuev, Ilya Makarov, Siyuan Wu, Yu-Chi Cheng, Yan-Ru Ju, Ti-Rong Wu, I-Hsuan Chu, Yu-Yu Yang, I-Chen Wu, Yitian Huang, Qinlu Cao, Yiheng Sun, Yuhong Dai, Hongkun Yao, Jingxuan Fu, Jiwei Zhang, Hao Liao, Mossimo Ebeling, Govind Arun, Sadhvik Bathini, Mihir S Arya, Avinash Anish, Aditya Ranjan, Kirtana Sunil Phatnani, Paval KS, Vrushali Mehta, Aravind S, Nikhil Arora, Tanya Upadhyay, Amol Bandagale, Yuan Lu, ChunEn Hsiao, YuTing Lin, Arvin Chung, Jerry John Thomas, Mathieu Laurière, Leshem Choshen, Yoram Bachrach, Pramod Viswanath, Maria Polukarov, Cheston Tan, Tal Kachman, Atlas Wang

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as interactive agents, yet their capacity for social and strategic reasoning over extended interaction remains poorly understood. Existing evaluations rely on static vignettes or single-game benchmarks that cannot capture the sustained, multi-faceted reasoning that real-world multi-agent settings demand. We introduce Mindgames, a multi-game arena and evaluation platform for LLM agents that operationalizes complementary reasoning demands relevant to ``theory of mind'': belief attribution under hidden information, opponent modeling through repeated strategic interaction, cooperative inference under knowledge asymmetries, and sustained deception in social deduction. Built on TextArena, Mindgames provides a unified interaction interface, TrueSkill-based rating, and full trajectory logging across four game environments. We instantiate Mindgames through a 2025 competition cycle hosted at a major AI conference, which assessed 944 submitted agents from 76 teams across four games: Colonel Blotto, Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma, Codenames, and Secret Mafia. Our analysis surfaces both agent-level and evaluation-level limitations: brittle rule adherence remains a major bottleneck, top-performing systems repeatedly rely on explicit structural scaffolding, and leaderboard validity differs sharply across environments. In particular, failure-heavy environments can reward robustness to opponent errors as much as strategic ability, with Secret Mafia exhibiting a pronounced error-survival confound in this cycle. We release a dataset of 29,571 multi-agent games with turn-level observations, actions, and rewards, together with MG-Ref, a deterministic offline tournament protocol that scores new agents against a frozen reference pool of top-ranked, low-error Stage~II submissions under the same error-attribution lens used in this analysis.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地被用作互動代理，但它們在長期互動中的社會和策略推理能力仍然不甚了解。現有的評估依賴於靜態短文或單一遊戲基準，無法捕捉現實世界多代理環境所需的持續、多面向的推理。我們推出了Mindgames，一個多遊戲競技場和評估平台，為LLM代理提供與「心智理論」相關的互補推理需求：在隱藏信息下的信念歸因、通過重複的策略互動進行對手建模、在知識不對稱下的合作推理，以及在社會推理中的持續欺騙。Mindgames基於TextArena構建，提供統一的互動介面、基於TrueSkill的評分以及四個遊戲環境中的完整軌跡記錄。我們通過在一個主要AI會議上舉辦的2025年競賽周期來實現Mindgames，該競賽評估了來自76個團隊的944個提交代理，涵蓋四個遊戲：Colonel Blotto、Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma、Codenames和Secret Mafia。我們的分析揭示了代理層面和評估層面的限制：脆弱的規則遵循仍然是一個主要瓶頸，表現最好的系統反覆依賴於明確的結構支架，且排行榜的有效性在不同環境中差異顯著。特別是，失敗頻繁的環境可以同樣獎勵對對手錯誤的魯棒性和策略能力，在這個周期中，Secret Mafia顯示出明顯的錯誤生存混淆。我們釋放了一個包含29,571場多代理遊戲的數據集，包含回合級觀察、行動和獎勵，以及MG-Ref，一個確定性的離線錦標賽協議，根據相同的錯誤歸因視角，對新的代理進行評分，與一個凍結的頂級低錯誤Stage~II提交的參考池進行比較。

##### **Quotient DAGs for Off-Policy Evaluation:Forward-Flow Importance Sampling and Exact Slate Propensities**
2605.29500v1 by Ziwen Xie, Shaowen Xiang, Hongyu He, Dianbo Liu

Off-policy evaluation estimates how a target policy would perform using data collected by a different behavior policy, which is crucial when online testing is costly or risky, such as in recommendation or healthcare. Standard importance sampling reweights each logged trajectory, but it can treat details of the generation process as meaningful even when the evaluation target ignores them: for example, an autoregressive slate recommender may generate an ordered sequence of items while the reward and downstream estimator depend only on the unordered slate. This creates nuisance variance and a computational gap, since exact unordered slate propensities require summing over all generation orders. We introduce a quotient-DAG view that merges histories equivalent for evaluation and assigns weights using target-to-behavior forward-flow ratios on the merged graph. For slate recommendation under a set-sufficient next-item interface, this yields Forward-DP, a subset-DAG dynamic program that computes exact unordered propensities without factorial enumeration. The resulting propensity primitive enables practical propensity-based evaluation and model selection for context-dependent autoregressive slate loggers.

摘要：Off-policy 評估估算目標策略在使用不同行為策略收集的數據下的表現，這在在線測試成本高或風險大的情況下至關重要，例如在推薦系統或醫療保健中。標準的重要性抽樣重新加權每個記錄的軌跡，但即使評估目標忽略這些細節，它仍然可以將生成過程的細節視為有意義的：例如，自回歸的清單推薦系統可能生成一個有序的項目序列，而獎勵和下游估計器僅依賴於無序的清單。這會產生干擾方差和計算差距，因為確切的無序清單傾向需要對所有生成順序進行求和。我們引入了一種商-DAG 視圖，將等效於評估的歷史合併，並在合併圖上使用目標到行為的前向流比率分配權重。對於在集合充分的下一項目介面下的清單推薦，這產生了 Forward-DP，一種子集-DAG 動態程序，可以在不進行階乘枚舉的情況下計算確切的無序傾向。生成的傾向原語使得基於傾向的實用評估和上下文依賴的自回歸清單記錄器的模型選擇成為可能。

##### **Composing Non-Conjugate Factor Graphs with Closed-Form Variational Inference**
2605.29467v1 by Mykola Lukashchuk, Kyrylo Yemets, Wouter M. Kouw, Dmitry Bagaev, İsmail Şenöz, Jeff Beck, Bert de Vries

Stacking probabilistic building blocks into deeper architectures typically breaks closed-form inference. We show that closed-form inference can be preserved. We identify five factor-graph primitives: a bilinear factor, an exponential link, a Gamma prior, a Gaussian likelihood, and an equality node, and prove that any model composed from them admits closed-form variational message passing. The construction works because each primitive preserves a small set of message families: under mean-field factorization, messages on Gaussian variables remain Gaussian and messages on precision variables remain Gamma, while the only non-conjugate interface, the exponential link, remains tractable through the Gaussian moment-generating function and the sufficient statistics of the Gamma family. We demonstrate composition at increasing depth, from static ensembles through input-dependent gating to split-branch routing, and show that stacking routing layers encodes arbitrary decision trees, establishing universal function approximation with closed-form inference. Applied to ensemble time-series forecasting, the framework yields a Bayesian mixture of experts in which gating functions are inferred rather than learned, providing calibrated uncertainty over expert selection across five benchmark datasets.

摘要：將概率建構塊堆疊成更深的架構通常會破壞閉式形式推斷。<lb/>我們展示了可以保留閉式形式推斷。<lb/>我們識別了五個因子圖原語：雙線性因子、指數連結、伽瑪先驗、高斯似然和等式節點，並證明了由它們組成的任何模型都承認閉式形式變異消息傳遞。<lb/>這一構造之所以有效，是因為每個原語保留了一小組消息族：在均值場因子化下，高斯變量上的消息保持高斯，而精度變量上的消息保持伽瑪，唯一的非共軛介面，即指數連結，則通過高斯矩生成函數和伽瑪族的充分統計量保持可處理性。<lb/>我們展示了在不斷增加的深度下的組合，從靜態集合到依賴輸入的閘控，再到分支路由，並顯示堆疊路由層編碼任意決策樹，確立了具有閉式形式推斷的通用函數逼近。<lb/>應用於集合時間序列預測，該框架產生了一個貝葉斯專家混合模型，其中閘控函數是推斷而不是學習的，提供了對五個基準數據集中的專家選擇的校準不確定性。

##### **Forget Less, Generalize More: Unifying Temporal and Structural Adaptation for Dynamic Graphs**
2605.29453v1 by Qian Chang, Ciprian Doru Giurcaneanu, Runsong Jia, Xia Li, Guoping Hu, Xiufeng Cheng, Jinqing Yang, Mengjia Wu, Yi Zhang

Representation learning on dynamic graphs requires capturing complex dependencies that evolve across both time and structure. Existing approaches typically adopt fixed temporal decay schemes or predetermined structural propagation depths, limiting their ability to generalize across graphs with diverse interaction frequencies and topological characteristics. We propose Dual-Scale Retentive Dynamics (DSRD), a unified framework that maintains a retentive representation state encoding both temporal memory and structural context. DSRD introduces two key components: (i) a retentive state with dual-scale adaptation that jointly models temporal dynamics and structural propagation within a single recurrent formulation, and (ii) adaptive decay kernels with learnable time-sensitivity parameters that automatically balance short-term responsiveness and long-term retention based on the underlying interaction patterns. We provide theoretical analysis establishing the equivalence between event-wise parallel aggregation and efficient recurrent state updates, as well as stability and boundedness guarantees for the learned dynamics. Extensive experiments on 14 real-world benchmarks demonstrate that DSRD consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance on both link prediction and node classification tasks, with strong generalization across transductive and inductive settings.

摘要：動態圖上的表示學習需要捕捉隨時間和結構演變的複雜依賴關係。現有的方法通常採用固定的時間衰減方案或預定的結構傳播深度，限制了它們在具有多樣互動頻率和拓撲特徵的圖上進行泛化的能力。我們提出了雙尺度保留動態（DSRD），這是一個統一框架，維持一個同時編碼時間記憶和結構上下文的保留表示狀態。DSRD引入了兩個關鍵組件：（i）具有雙尺度適應的保留狀態，該狀態在單一的遞歸公式中共同建模時間動態和結構傳播，以及（ii）具有可學習時間敏感參數的自適應衰減核，這些核根據潛在的互動模式自動平衡短期反應能力和長期保留。 我們提供了理論分析，確立事件級並行聚合與高效遞歸狀態更新之間的等價性，以及對學習動態的穩定性和有界性保證。在14個現實世界基準上的廣泛實驗表明，DSRD在鏈接預測和節點分類任務上始終達到最先進的性能，並在傳導和誘導設置中具有強大的泛化能力。

##### **FinGuard: Detecting Financial Regulatory Non-Compliance in LLM Interactions**
2605.29427v1 by Huaixia Dou, Jie Zhu, Minghao Wu, Shuo Jiang, Junhui Li, Lifan Guo, Feng Chen, Chi Zhang

As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in financial services, a single non-compliant interaction can expose institutions to regulatory penalties and direct consumer harm. We address this gap with a regulation-driven pipeline that operates directly on regulatory documents, inducing a financial compliance risk taxonomy and synthesizing grounded training data without any predefined violation categories. ##### **Learning Design Skills as Memory Policies for Agentic Photonic Inverse Design**
2605.29421v1 by Shengchao Chen, Ting Shu, Sufen Ren

Photonic crystal fiber (PCF) inverse design remains challenging because candidate geometries must satisfy coupled optical targets under expensive electromagnetic simulation. Existing pipelines improve surrogate prediction or one-shot parameter recommendation, but they do not accumulate reusable design knowledge across iterative trials. ##### **EvoMD-LLM: Learning the Language of Species Evolution in Reactive Molecular Dynamics**
2605.29394v1 by Zhichen Tang, Zhengzheng Dang, Yulin Chen, Jixin Wu, Haiwen Li, Yanming Wang

While large language models (LLMs) excel at static scientific reasoning, they struggle to model the temporal structure of dynamic physical processes. We present EvoMD-LLM (Evolutionary Molecular Dynamics Large Language Model), a framework that reformulates species-level molecular dynamics as a symbolic temporal language modeling problem. Reactive MD trajectories are discretized into sequences of molecular events, where each token represents a chemical species augmented with its persistence duration, enabling standard autoregressive LLMs to learn compositional evolution over time through efficient fine-tuning. A key component of EvoMD-LLM is temporal scaffolding, which treats event duration as an explicit linguistic token and serves as a structured inductive bias, significantly reducing invalid or hallucinated molecular outputs compared to conventional sequence modeling approaches. We evaluate EvoMD-LLM on multiple temporal prediction tasks, achieving up to 66.14% accuracy and consistently outperforming sequential neural networks and language-based baselines. Beyond quantitative improvements, we qualitatively observe that the model is capable of generating interpretations for its own predictions by incorporating relevant chemical knowledge, even though it was not explicitly supervised with paired trajectory-explanation data. These results demonstrate that symbolic temporal language modeling provides an effective framework for grounding LLMs in dynamic physical simulations.

摘要：雖然大型語言模型（LLMs）在靜態科學推理方面表現優異，但它們在建模動態物理過程的時間結構上卻面臨挑戰。<lb/>我們提出了EvoMD-LLM（進化分子動力學大型語言模型），這是一個將物種級別的分子動力學重新表述為符號時間語言建模問題的框架。<lb/>反應性MD軌跡被離散化為分子事件的序列，其中每個標記代表一種化學物質，並附加其持續時間，使得標準自回歸LLMs能夠通過高效的微調學習隨時間的組合演變。<lb/>EvoMD-LLM的一個關鍵組件是時間支架，它將事件持續時間視為一個明確的語言標記，並作為一種結構化的歸納偏差，顯著減少了與傳統序列建模方法相比的無效或幻覺的分子輸出。<lb/>我們在多個時間預測任務上評估EvoMD-LLM，達到高達66.14%的準確率，並始終超越序列神經網絡和基於語言的基準。<lb/>除了定量改進外，我們還質性地觀察到該模型能夠通過結合相關的化學知識生成對其自身預測的解釋，即使它並未明確地用配對的軌跡-解釋數據進行監督。<lb/>這些結果表明，符號時間語言建模為將LLMs根植於動態物理模擬提供了一個有效的框架。

##### **TRACER: Persistent Regularization for Robust Multimodal Finetuning**
2605.29380v1 by Hesam Asadollahzadeh, Feng Liu, Christopher Leckie, Sarah M. Erfani

Mainstream strategies for finetuning pretrained multimodal models often degrade out-of-distribution (OOD) robustness, a phenomenon known as catastrophic forgetting. In this paper, we develop a theoretical framework for multimodal contrastive finetuning, yielding closed-form solutions and a geometric decomposition for each strategy. This framework shows that self-distillation is more effective than other regularization approaches to retain the knowledge of the pretrained model. Our analysis reveals a largely overlooked limitation: standard Exponential Moving Average (EMA) teachers, widely used in robust finetuning, suffer from collapse. To solve this, we prove that a Weighted Moving Average (WMA) teacher maintains a persistent regularizing force over finite horizons and yields bias-free convergence in the task subspace while preserving orthogonal knowledge. These insights motivate **TRACER** (**T**rajectory-**R**obust **A**nchoring for **C**ontrastive **E**ncoder **R**egularization), which combines contrastive learning with WMA-guided multi-perspective distillation. Extensive experiments on CLIP finetuning demonstrate consistent OOD accuracy and calibration gains across three backbone architectures, and comprehensive ablations confirm that TRACER is both principled and robust to hyperparameter choices. Code is available at [https://github.com/HesamAsad/TRACER](https://github.com/HesamAsad/TRACER).

摘要：主流的微調預訓練多模態模型的策略往往會降低對分佈外（OOD）穩健性的強度，這一現象被稱為災難性遺忘。<lb/>在本文中，我們開發了一個多模態對比微調的理論框架，為每種策略提供了封閉形式的解和幾何分解。<lb/>這個框架顯示，自我蒸餾比其他正則化方法更有效地保留預訓練模型的知識。<lb/>我們的分析揭示了一個被大多數人忽視的限制：標準的指數移動平均（EMA）教師在穩健微調中廣泛使用，但卻遭遇崩潰。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們證明加權移動平均（WMA）教師在有限的時間範圍內保持持久的正則化力量，並在任務子空間中實現無偏收斂，同時保留正交知識。<lb/>這些見解促使了**TRACER**（**T**rajectory-**R**obust **A**nchoring for **C**ontrastive **E**ncoder **R**egularization）的誕生，它將對比學習與WMA引導的多視角蒸餾相結合。<lb/>在CLIP微調上的廣泛實驗顯示，三種主幹架構的一致OOD準確性和校準增益，並且全面的消融實驗確認TRACER在超參數選擇上既有原則性又穩健。<lb/>代碼可在[https://github.com/HesamAsad/TRACER](https://github.com/HesamAsad/TRACER)獲得。

##### **PassNet: Scaling Large Language Models for Graph Compiler Pass Generation**
2605.29357v1 by Yiqun Liu, Yingsheng Wu, Ruqi Yang, Enrong Zheng, Honglei Qiu, Sijun He, Tai Liang, Jingjing Wu, Yuhan Zhou, Yiwei Zhang, Dongyan Chen, Weihan Yi, Xinqi Li, Siqi Bao

Modern tensor compilers such as TorchInductor deliver substantial speedups on mainstream models, yet face a systematic performance ceiling on long-tail workloads -- our profiling shows that 43% of real-world subgraphs experience end-to-end slowdowns under default compilation. While LLMs offer a path toward automated optimization, existing efforts focus on standalone kernel generation. We argue that pass generation -- where LLMs author structured graph transformations that integrate directly into compiler pipelines -- is the more appropriate abstraction. We propose PassNet, the first large-scale ecosystem for LLM-based compiler pass generation, comprising: (1) PassNet-Dataset, over 18K unique computational graphs from 100K real-world models; and (2) PassBench, 200 curated long-tail fusible tasks (comprising 2,060 subgraphs in total) evaluated under the Error-aware Speedup Score (ES_t) -- a metric unifying correctness, stability, and performance -- with layered integrity defenses against systematic LLM exploitation. Experiments reveal that PassBench is both highly discriminative and genuinely unsaturated: the best frontier model trails TorchInductor by 37% in aggregate, yet on individual subgraphs LLMs achieve up to 3x speedup over the same compiler -- indicating that the bottleneck is consistency, not capability. Fine-tuning a small model on merely ~4K PassNet trajectories yields a 2.67x improvement approaching frontier-model performance, demonstrating substantial headroom and validating PassNet as live training infrastructure for advancing LLM-driven compiler optimization. All data, benchmarks, and tooling are publicly available.

摘要：現代的張量編譯器，如 TorchInductor，在主流模型上提供了顯著的加速，但在長尾工作負載上面臨系統性的性能瓶頸——我們的分析顯示，43% 的真實子圖在默認編譯下經歷了端到端的減速。雖然 LLM 提供了一條自動優化的途徑，但現有的努力集中在獨立的內核生成上。我們認為，通過生成——即 LLM 編寫結構化圖變換，這些變換直接整合到編譯器管道中——是更合適的抽象。我們提出了 PassNet，首個基於 LLM 的編譯器通過生成的大規模生態系統，包括：(1) PassNet-Dataset，來自 100K 真實模型的超過 18K 獨特計算圖；以及 (2) PassBench，200 個策劃的長尾可融合任務（共包括 2,060 個子圖），在錯誤感知加速分數（ES_t）下進行評估——這是一個統一正確性、穩定性和性能的指標——並針對系統性 LLM 利用設計了分層的完整性防禦。實驗顯示，PassBench 既具有高度的區分性，又真正未飽和：最佳前沿模型在總體上落後於 TorchInductor 37%，但在個別子圖上，LLM 在同一編譯器上實現了高達 3 倍的加速——這表明瓶頸在於一致性，而非能力。僅在約 4K PassNet 軌跡上微調一個小模型即可實現 2.67 倍的改進，接近前沿模型的性能，顯示出顯著的提升空間，並驗證了 PassNet 作為推進 LLM 驅動編譯器優化的實時訓練基礎設施。所有數據、基準和工具均可公開獲得。

##### **GrepSeek: Training Search Agents for Direct Corpus Interaction**
2605.29307v1 by Alireza Salemi, Chang Zeng, Atharva Nijasure, Jui-Hui Chung, Razieh Rahimi, Fernando Diaz, Hamed Zamani

Large Language Model (LLM) search agents have shown strong promise for knowledge-intensive language tasks through multiple rounds of reasoning and information retrieval. Most existing systems access information using a retriever that takes a keyword or natural language query and returns a ranked list of documents using an index of pre-computed document representations. In this work, we explore a complementary perspective in which the search agent treats the corpus itself as the search environment and finds evidence by issuing executable shell commands. We introduce GrepSeek, an optimized direct corpus interaction (DCI) search agent that trains a compact search agent to find, filter, and compose evidence from large text corpora. To address the instability of learning behavior directly with reinforcement learning on large corpora, we propose a two-stage training pipeline. First, we construct a cold-start dataset using an answer-aware Tutor and answer-blind Planner to generate verified, causally grounded search trajectories. Second, we refine the initialized policy with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), allowing the agent to improve its task-oriented search behavior through direct interaction with the corpus. To make DCI practical at scale, we further use a semantics-preserving sharded-parallel execution engine that accelerates shell-based retrieval by up to $7.6\times$ while preserving byte-exact equivalence with sequential execution of the shell command. Experiments across seven open-domain question answering benchmarks show that GrepSeek achieves the strongest overall token-level $F_1$ and Exact Match. Our analysis also highlights the limitations of purely lexical interaction on queries with substantial surface-form variation, suggesting DCI as a practical and competitive method for search agents that can complement existing retrieval paradigms in the real world.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLM）搜索代理在知識密集型語言任務中通過多輪推理和信息檢索顯示出強大的潛力。大多數現有系統使用檢索器訪問信息，該檢索器接受關鍵字或自然語言查詢，並使用預先計算的文檔表示索引返回一個排名文檔列表。在這項工作中，我們探索了一種互補的視角，其中搜索代理將語料庫本身視為搜索環境，並通過發出可執行的 shell 命令來尋找證據。我們介紹了 GrepSeek，一個優化的直接語料互動（DCI）搜索代理，該代理訓練一個緊湊的搜索代理來查找、過濾和組合來自大型文本語料庫的證據。為了解決在大型語料庫上直接使用強化學習學習行為的不穩定性，我們提出了一個兩階段的訓練管道。首先，我們使用一個關注答案的導師和一個不關注答案的規劃者構建一個冷啟動數據集，以生成經過驗證的、因果基礎的搜索軌跡。其次，我們使用群體相對策略優化（GRPO）來細化初始化的策略，允許代理通過與語料庫的直接互動來改進其以任務為導向的搜索行為。為了使 DCI 在規模上實用，我們進一步使用一個保持語義的分片並行執行引擎，該引擎在保持與 shell 命令的順序執行的字節精確等價的同時，加速基於 shell 的檢索速度高達 $7.6\times$。在七個開放領域問答基準上的實驗顯示，GrepSeek 在整體標記級別的 $F_1$ 和精確匹配上達到了最強的表現。我們的分析還突顯了在表面形式變化顯著的查詢上純粹詞彙互動的局限性，這表明 DCI 是一種實用且具有競爭力的方法，可以補充現有的檢索範式於現實世界中。

##### **Entropy-KL Divergence-based Token Masking: A Novel Approach for Selective Fine-tuning of Large Language Models**
2605.29303v1 by Qi Liu, Mingdi Sun, Yongyi He, Zhi Zheng, Tong Xu, Yi Zheng, Zhefeng Wang, Enhong Chen

Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) followed by reinforcement learning (RL) has become a standard post-training paradigm for large language models. This paradigm provides a cold-start for RL exploration, avoiding the inefficiency of pure RL where on-policy sampling yields insufficient positive samples. However, in practice, existing approaches often use a small amount of data for SFT initialization compared to the RL phase, which can cause the model to fit the limited samples and shift away from its pre-trained distribution. This distribution shift impedes the model's ability to effectively explore during subsequent RL training. To address this challenge, we propose that in low-data regimes, SFT should prioritize activating task-relevant capabilities rather than memorizing specific content. Along this line, we propose EKSFT (Entropy-KL Selective Fine-Tuning), which selectively masks tokens that exhibit either high entropy or high KL divergence from a reference model. By excluding these high-uncertainty, distribution-shifting tokens from imitation, EKSFT injects task-specific knowledge while preserving the integrity of the model's pre-trained distribution. Empirical evaluations on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that EKSFT consistently outperforms standard SFT. Further RL fine-tuning from the EKSFT model yields consistently better post-RL performance, indicating improved exploration for the RL stage. Our codes and datasets are available at https://github.com/MINE-USTC/EKSFT.

摘要：監督微調（SFT）隨後進行強化學習（RL）已成為大型語言模型的標準後訓練範式。<lb/>這一範式為RL探索提供了冷啟動，避免了純RL中由於策略採樣產生的正樣本不足的低效率。<lb/>然而，在實踐中，現有的方法通常在SFT初始化階段使用的數據量相對於RL階段來說較少，這可能導致模型擬合有限的樣本並偏離其預訓練的分佈。<lb/>這種分佈偏移妨礙了模型在隨後RL訓練中有效探索的能力。<lb/>為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出在低數據環境下，SFT應優先激活與任務相關的能力，而不是記憶特定內容。<lb/>沿著這一思路，我們提出了EKSFT（熵-KL選擇性微調），該方法選擇性地屏蔽那些顯示出高熵或高KL散度的標記，這些標記來自參考模型。<lb/>通過排除這些高不確定性、分佈偏移的標記，EKSFT在保留模型預訓練分佈的完整性的同時注入了任務特定的知識。<lb/>在數學推理基準上的實證評估顯示，EKSFT始終優於標準SFT。<lb/>從EKSFT模型進行的進一步RL微調產生了一致更好的後RL性能，表明在RL階段的探索能力有所改善。<lb/>我們的代碼和數據集可在 https://github.com/MINE-USTC/EKSFT 獲得。

##### **Do Physics Foundation Models Learn Generalizable Physics? A Bias-Aware Benchmark Across Physical Regimes and Distribution Shifts**
2605.29283v1 by Mengdi Chu, Yang Liu, Ayan Biswas, Han-Wei Shen

Recent physics foundation models claim general spatiotemporal forecasting ability, yet their evaluations often collapse performance into a single average score under a fixed training distribution. This makes it difficult to determine whether a model has learned generalizable physical dynamics or only performs well under particular settings. We construct a benchmark with 8 physical dynamics, 3 training-data mixtures, and 25 test regimes induced by dynamic-scale and initial-condition complexity shifts, covering in-distribution, distribution-shift, and out-of-distribution settings. We evaluate five physics foundation model architectures and four model variants per architecture (scratch and three pretrained sizes), resulting in 60,000 measurements. Our results show that current physics foundation models behave as conditional rather than universal generalists: their generality depends on the physical regime, temporal scale, initial-condition setting, pretraining, model size, and architecture. Improving the training data distribution only partially mitigates this limitation. Pretraining and scaling are also unable to reliably remove their ability biases. We argue that improving physics foundation models requires moving beyond scaling models or expanding data, toward learning mechanisms that better capture transferable physical knowledge across regimes, temporal scales, and distribution shifts.

摘要：最近的物理基礎模型聲稱具有一般的時空預測能力，然而它們的評估常常將性能壓縮為在固定訓練分佈下的單一平均分數。這使得難以確定模型是否學會了可泛化的物理動力學，或者僅僅是在特定設置下表現良好。我們構建了一個基準，包含 8 種物理動力學、3 種訓練數據混合以及 25 種由動態尺度和初始條件複雜度變化引起的測試方案，涵蓋了內部分佈、分佈轉移和外部分佈設置。我們評估了五種物理基礎模型架構以及每種架構的四種模型變體（從頭開始和三種預訓練大小），總共進行了 60,000 次測量。我們的結果顯示，當前的物理基礎模型表現為條件性而非普遍性通才：它們的普遍性依賴於物理範疇、時間尺度、初始條件設置、預訓練、模型大小和架構。改善訓練數據分佈僅部分減輕了這一限制。預訓練和擴展也無法可靠地消除它們的能力偏差。我們認為，改善物理基礎模型需要超越擴展模型或擴大數據，朝著學習更好捕捉跨範疇、時間尺度和分佈轉移的可轉移物理知識的機制邁進。

##### **LoopFM: Learning frOm HistOrical RePresentations of Foundation Model for Recommendation**
2605.29280v1 by Shali Jiang, Hua Zheng, Boyang Liu, Laming Chen, Kenny Lov, Chuanqi Xu, Lisang Ding, Qinghai Zhou, Can Cui, Xiaolong Liu, Xiaoyi Liu, Yasmine Badr, Xin Xu, Jiyan Yang, Ellie Dingqiao Wen, Gerard Jonathan Mugisha Akkerhuis, Chenxiao Guan, Rong Jin, Ruichao Qiu, Xian Chen, Shifu Xu, Zhehui Zhou, Ping Chen, Rui Yang, Haicheng Chen, Xiangge Meng, Song Zhou, Dharak Kharod, Shuyu Xu, Qiang Jin, Qiao Yang, Wankun Zhu, Qin Huang, Yuzhen Huang, Darren Liu, Parish Aggarwal, Hui Zhou, Erzhuo Wang, Shuo Chang, Xiaorui Gan, Wenlin Chen, Santanu Kolay, Huayu Li

Knowledge distillation (KD) transfers a single scalar prediction from a large foundation model (FM) to compact vertical models (VMs), suffering from diminishing transfer ratio -- the fraction of FM improvement captured by the VM -- as a single scalar cannot convey the rich intermediate knowledge that larger FMs learn. To address this bottleneck, we propose LoopFM (Learning frOm HistOrical ReP*resentations of FM), a framework that opens a high-bandwidth transfer channel by structuring FM intermediate embeddings as input features (e.g., user history sequence) for downstream VMs, without requiring real-time FM inference at serving and architectural coupling between FM and VM. We provide a theoretical framework for LoopFM with a gain decomposition and transfer-ratio analysis. On three public benchmarks, LoopFM demonstrates strong AUC improvements (e.g., 6\%+ on TaobaoAd) and complementary knowledge transfer capability with KD. On industrial-scale systems (billions of examples, trillion-parameter FMs), LoopFM approximately doubles the knowledge transfer ratio on top of KD, delivering a +0.5\% conversion improvement in Y1H1, and a +1.03\% and +1.22\% conversion improvement from two individual launches respectively in Y1H2.

摘要：知識蒸餾 (KD) 將大型基礎模型 (FM) 的單一標量預測轉移至緊湊的垂直模型 (VMs)，但面臨轉移比率下降的問題——即 VM 捕捉到的 FM 改進的比例——因為單一標量無法傳達較大 FM 所學習的豐富中間知識。為了解決這一瓶頸，我們提出了 LoopFM（來自 FM 的歷史表示學習），這是一個通過將 FM 的中間嵌入結構化為下游 VMs 的輸入特徵（例如，用戶歷史序列）來開啟高帶寬轉移通道的框架，而不需要在服務時進行實時的 FM 推理或 FM 與 VM 之間的架構耦合。我們為 LoopFM 提供了一個理論框架，包含增益分解和轉移比率分析。在三個公共基準測試中，LoopFM 顯示出強勁的 AUC 改進（例如，在 TaobaoAd 上增長 6\%+）以及與 KD 的互補知識轉移能力。在工業規模系統（數十億個例子，萬億參數的 FM）上，LoopFM 在 KD 的基礎上大約將知識轉移比率翻倍，在 Y1H1 中實現了 +0.5\% 的轉換改進，並在 Y1H2 中分別從兩次單獨的啟動中實現了 +1.03\% 和 +1.22\% 的轉換改進。

##### **Learnable Assessment Skills for LLM-based Automated Scoring: Rubric Construction via Iterative Optimization**
2605.29274v1 by Yun Wang, Xin Xia, Xuansheng Wu, Xiaoming Zhai, Ninghao Liu

LLM-based automated scoring approaches near-human performance, but scaling to new tasks remains bottlenecked by the per-item human configuration of upstream stages such as rubric construction. Human experts bypass this bottleneck through evaluation heuristics developed over extensive practice. We ask whether LLMs can learn similar heuristics directly from scoring experience, and formalize this as the concept of assessment skills: item-independent natural-language procedural knowledge that guides LLMs through specific stages of the scoring workflow. Focusing on rubric construction as a first instantiation, we propose an iterative framework that decomposes a skill into a fixed scaffold and learnable item-agnostic rules, refining the rules through LLM-driven diagnosis of scoring errors and validation-gated selection. The framework requires no expert-written rubric. On all ten ASAP-SAS items, optimized skills substantially improve LLM-based scoring and frequently surpass the dataset-provided expert rubric. 摘要：LLM 基礎的自動評分方法接近人類表現，但擴展到新任務仍然受到如評分標準構建等上游階段每項目人類配置的瓶頸。人類專家通過在廣泛實踐中發展的評估啟發式方法來繞過這一瓶頸。我們詢問 LLM 是否能夠直接從評分經驗中學習類似的啟發式，並將其形式化為評估技能的概念：獨立於項目的自然語言程序知識，指導 LLM 通過評分工作流程的特定階段。以評分標準構建作為第一個具體實例，我們提出了一個迭代框架，將技能分解為固定的支架和可學習的項目無關規則，通過 LLM 驅動的評分錯誤診斷和驗證門控選擇來完善這些規則。該框架不需要專家編寫的評分標準。在所有十個 ASAP-SAS 項目中，優化的技能顯著改善了基於 LLM 的評分，並且經常超過數據集提供的專家評分標準。跨項目轉移實驗進一步顯示，學習到的技能捕捉了可泛化和項目特定的模式。

##### **OmniRetrieval: Unified Retrieval across Heterogeneous Knowledge Sources**
2605.29250v1 by Jinheon Baek, Soyeong Jeong, Sangwoo Park, Woongyeong Yeo, Minki Kang, Patara Trirat, Heejun Lee, Sung Ju Hwang

Real-world information needs require access to structurally diverse knowledge sources, from unstructured text and relational tables to knowledge graphs and property graphs. Existing retrievers, however, operate over one source at a time under a fixed query language, leaving the broader landscape of available knowledge fragmented behind incompatible interfaces. A natural attempt at unification would collapse these sources into a shared space, but this erases the structural affordances (such as schemas, ontologies, compositional operators) that give each source its expressive power. Effective retrieval over diverse knowledge, therefore, requires not homogenization but an overarching layer that meets each source on its own terms. To achieve this, we present OmniRetrieval, a framework that takes any natural-language query, identifies appropriate knowledge sources, and dispatches source-native queries to their native execution engines. Across an extensive benchmark spanning 13 datasets and 309 distinct knowledge bases over text, relational, and graph-structured sources, OmniRetrieval exceeds single-source baselines, demonstrating that it can serve as a general-purpose interface to the heterogeneous sources while preserving the structural distinctions that make each source valuable.

摘要：現實世界的信息需求需要訪問結構多樣的知識來源，從非結構化文本和關聯表到知識圖和屬性圖。然而，現有的檢索器在固定查詢語言下一次只對一個來源進行操作，這使得可用知識的更廣泛景觀在不兼容的界面後變得支離破碎。自然的統一嘗試會將這些來源合併到一個共享空間中，但這會抹去結構性優勢（例如模式、本體、組合運算符），使每個來源失去其表達力。因此，對多樣化知識的有效檢索需要的不是同質化，而是一個總體層面，以各自的條件滿足每個來源。為了實現這一點，我們提出了OmniRetrieval，一個框架，它接受任何自然語言查詢，識別適當的知識來源，並將來源本地查詢發送到其本地執行引擎。在涵蓋13個數據集和309個不同知識庫的廣泛基準測試中，OmniRetrieval超越了單一來源的基準，證明它可以作為異質來源的通用接口，同時保留使每個來源有價值的結構區別。

##### **GTA: Generating Long-Horizon Tasks for Web Agents at Scale**
2605.29218v1 by Tenghao Huang, Kung-Hsiang Huang, Prafulla Kumar Choubey, Yilun Zhou, Muhao Chen, Jonathan May, Chien-Sheng Wu

Web agents, which couple language models with browsing and tool-use capabilities, show promise as open web assistants. Yet progress is increasingly limited by the lack of scalable, process-level supervision. Existing benchmarks are largely manually constructed, providing only coarse start-goal annotations without intermediate trajectories, while recent automatic generation efforts remain expensive, biased, and shallow. These limitations prevent reliable training and evaluation of agents that must generalize to realistic, multi-hop, cross-page tasks. We introduce a scalable framework, GTA, that integrates crawling, retrieval-based seeding, in-context generation, and automated quality control to produce realistic tasks paired with executable trajectories. This design decouples crawling from generation for greater efficiency, grounds tasks in the site graph to enforce compositionality, and ensures dense supervision through deterministic replays and systematic validation.
