##### **Better Later Than Sooner: Neuro-Symbolic Knowledge Graph Construction via Ontology-grounded Post-extraction Correction**
2605.29168v1 by Lorenzo Loconte, Timothy Hospedales, Cristina Cornelio

Question answering (QA) is a core challenge in AI, particularly for complex queries requiring multi-hop reasoning across documents, or symbolic operations like aggregation or exhaustive listing. Retrieval-augmented generation has become the dominant approach to QA, with recent graph-based variants addressing part of these issues by organizing knowledge to better support compositional questions. However, most textual graph-based RAG methods still lack the structure needed for symbolic operations useful to answer complex questions reliably. This motivates symbolic graph-based approaches, which extract knowledge graphs (KGs) whose relations are logic predicates that enable SQL-like querying. Yet these pipelines typically use LLMs for KG extraction, which can introduce consistency issues, where extracted facts may violate commonsense ontology constraints. We propose a neuro-symbolic framework for ontology-grounded KG construction combining open-domain extraction, embedding-based canonicalization of types and predicates, and targeted LLM-based correction of ontology violations. By deferring corrections to a post-extraction stage, our method avoids repeated LLM calls, substantially reducing token usage while improving KG consistency and preserving downstream QA quality. Finally, we show that the extracted KGs are well suited for symbolic querying by measuring the occurrence of SPARQL graph patterns.

摘要：問題回答（QA）是人工智慧中的核心挑戰，特別是對於需要跨文件進行多跳推理的複雜查詢，或像聚合或徹底列舉這樣的符號操作。檢索增強生成已成為QA的主導方法，最近的基於圖形的變體通過組織知識來更好地支持組合問題，解決了這些問題的一部分。然而，大多數基於文本的圖形RAG方法仍然缺乏進行符號操作所需的結構，以可靠地回答複雜問題。這促使了符號圖形基礎的方法，這些方法提取知識圖（KG），其關係是邏輯謂詞，使得類似SQL的查詢成為可能。然而，這些管道通常使用LLM進行KG提取，這可能引入一致性問題，提取的事實可能違反常識本體約束。我們提出了一個神經符號框架，用於基於本體的KG構建，結合了開放域提取、基於嵌入的類型和謂詞的標準化，以及針對本體違規的有針對性的LLM修正。通過將修正推遲到提取後階段，我們的方法避免了重複的LLM調用，顯著減少了標記使用，同時提高了KG的一致性並保持了下游QA的質量。最後，我們通過測量SPARQL圖模式的出現來顯示提取的KG非常適合符號查詢。

##### **Evolutionary Refinement of Generative Graph Topologies: A Hybrid WGAN-GA Approach**
2605.29161v1 by James Sargant, Seyedeh Ava Razi Razavi, Renata Dividino, Sheridan Houghten

Generating realistic graph-structured data is challenging due to discrete connectivity, varying graph sizes, and class-specific structural patterns. Recent Generative Adversarial Networks (GAN)-based graph generation methods improve edge modelling by learning connectivity and matching class-specific density distributions. However these models still exhibit noticeable deviations such as in degree and spectral distribution when compared to real graphs, indicating that important structural properties are not fully preserved. This work aims to reduce these deviations by refining the graphs produced by an existing GAN-based graph generator framework with a Genetic Algorithm (GA). In the GAN framework, the generator produces both node features and connectivity patterns, while a GNN-based critic evaluates graph realism and class consistency to ensure global structural and class alignment. Building on this foundation, we apply a GA to refine the edges of generated graphs. The refinement process guides synthetic graphs toward closer agreement with real data, while preserving diversity and novelty. Experimental results show that the GA refinement consistently lowers combined Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD) compared to the base model, leading to graphs that more closely match real structural patterns. This demonstrates that evolutionary refinement is an effective and flexible way to correct residual structural deviations in GAN-based graph generators, improving their suitability for realistic graph synthesis and data augmentation.

摘要：生成現實的圖形結構數據是具有挑戰性的，因為存在離散的連接性、變化的圖形大小和特定類別的結構模式。最近基於生成對抗網絡（GAN）的圖形生成方法通過學習連接性和匹配特定類別的密度分佈來改善邊緣建模。然而，這些模型在與真實圖形相比時，仍然顯示出明顯的偏差，例如在度數和頻譜分佈方面，這表明重要的結構特性並未完全保留。本研究旨在通過使用遺傳算法（GA）來精煉現有基於GAN的圖形生成器框架所產生的圖形，以減少這些偏差。在GAN框架中，生成器同時產生節點特徵和連接模式，而基於GNN的評價者則評估圖形的真實性和類別一致性，以確保全局結構和類別的對齊。在此基礎上，我們應用GA來精煉生成圖形的邊緣。精煉過程指導合成圖形朝向與真實數據更接近的協調，同時保持多樣性和新穎性。實驗結果顯示，與基礎模型相比，GA精煉始終能降低綜合最大均值差異（MMD），從而生成更接近真實結構模式的圖形。這表明，進化精煉是一種有效且靈活的方法，可以修正基於GAN的圖形生成器中的殘餘結構偏差，提高其對現實圖形合成和數據增強的適用性。

##### **Parallax: Parameterized Local Linear Attention for Language Modeling**
2605.29157v1 by Yifei Zuo, Dhruv Pai, Zhichen Zeng, Alec Dewulf, Shuming Hu, Zhaoran Wang

Large Language Models (LLMs) have become the central paradigm in artificial intelligence, yet the core computational primitive of attention has remained structurally unchanged. Local Linear Attention (LLA) is an attention mechanism derived from nonparametric statistics in the test-time regression framework. In contrast to prior research on efficient attention variants, LLA upgrades the local constant estimate in softmax attention to a local linear estimate, yielding provably superior bias-variance tradeoffs for associative memory. However, LLA has not been scaled in LLM pretraining due to computational and numerical stability concerns. We introduce Parallax, a parameterized Local Linear Attention that is scalable for LLMs. Parallax eliminates the numerical solver in LLA and learns an extra query-like projector that probes the KV covariance. We place Parallax within a family of attention mechanisms connected by the bandwidth, the probe construction and the affine structure. We propose a hardware-aware algorithm that increases the arithmetic intensity over FlashAttention, shifting attention into a more compute bound regime. Our prototype decode kernel matches or outperforms FlashAttention 2/3 across diverse batch sizes and context lengths. We pretrain Parallax at 0.6B and 1.7B scales and find consistent perplexity improvements throughout pretraining with gains that transfer to downstream benchmarks. The advantage persists under both parameter-matched and compute-matched controls, demonstrating a Pareto improvement. We perform careful pretraining ablations and identify a novel phenomenon whereby Muon unlocks the capacity of Parallax. To our knowledge, this is the first empirical demonstration of strong architecture-optimizer codesign for attention mechanisms in the architecture research literature.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）已成為人工智慧的核心範式，但注意力的核心計算原語仍然在結構上保持不變。局部線性注意力（LLA）是一種源自於非參數統計的注意力機制，應用於測試時回歸框架。與先前對高效注意力變體的研究相比，LLA 將 softmax 注意力中的局部常數估計升級為局部線性估計，從而為聯想記憶提供可證明的更優偏差-方差權衡。然而，由於計算和數值穩定性問題，LLA 尚未在 LLM 預訓練中擴展。我們引入 Parallax，一種可擴展的參數化局部線性注意力，適用於 LLM。Parallax 消除了 LLA 中的數值求解器，並學習了一個額外的類查詢投影器，用於探測 KV 協方差。我們將 Parallax 放置在一個由帶寬、探測器構造和仿射結構相連的注意力機制家族中。我們提出了一種硬體感知算法，增加了相較於 FlashAttention 的算術強度，將注意力轉移到更計算密集的範疇。我們的原型解碼內核在不同的批次大小和上下文長度下與 FlashAttention 2/3 匹配或超越。我們在 0.6B 和 1.7B 的規模上預訓練 Parallax，並發現在整個預訓練過程中一致的困惑度改善，這些增益可轉移到下游基準。這一優勢在參數匹配和計算匹配的控制下持續存在，顯示出 Pareto 改進。我們進行了仔細的預訓練消融實驗，並識別出一種新現象，即 Muon 解鎖了 Parallax 的容量。據我們所知，這是架構研究文獻中對注意力機制進行強架構-優化器共同設計的首次實證展示。

##### **SafeRx-Agent: A Knowledge-Grounded Multi-Agent Framework for Safe and Explainable Medication Recommendation**
2605.29146v1 by Xinyu Wang, Hanwei Wu, Zhenghan Tai, Sicheng Lyu, Qincheng Lu, Ziyu Zhao, Jijun Chi, Jingrui Tian, Xiao-Wen Chang, Ziyang Song

Medication recommendation predicts medications for patient visits, but existing methods still face two key challenges. At the model level, traditional drug recommendation methods only predict structured drug codes with limited evidence grounding, while LLM agents can use richer clinical context but may lack safety verification and traceability. At the task level, existing benchmarks often use broad medication categories, which ignore subgroup-level safety differences and can lead to risk overestimation. We introduce the first fine-grained medication recommendation setting based on fourth-level ATC code generation. We propose Safe Prescription Agent (SafeRx-Agent), a knowledge-grounded multi-agent framework that uses patient context, external clinical knowledge, and safety verification to recommend traceable medication sets. Experimental results on MIMIC-III and MIMIC-IV datasets show that SafeRx-Agent improves fine-grained medication prediction accuracy while controlling drug interactions, contraindications, and medication set size.

摘要：藥物推薦預測患者就診的藥物，但現有方法仍面臨兩個主要挑戰。在模型層面，傳統的藥物推薦方法僅預測結構化的藥物代碼，且證據基礎有限，而大型語言模型（LLM）代理可以使用更豐富的臨床背景，但可能缺乏安全性驗證和可追溯性。在任務層面，現有基準通常使用廣泛的藥物類別，這忽略了亞組層級的安全性差異，並可能導致風險的高估。我們引入了第一個基於第四級ATC代碼生成的細粒度藥物推薦設置。我們提出了安全處方代理（SafeRx-Agent），這是一個知識驅動的多代理框架，利用患者背景、外部臨床知識和安全性驗證來推薦可追溯的藥物集。在MIMIC-III和MIMIC-IV數據集上的實驗結果顯示，SafeRx-Agent在控制藥物相互作用、禁忌症和藥物集大小的同時，提高了細粒度藥物預測的準確性。

##### **The Importance of Out-of-Band Metadata for Safe Autonomous Agents: The Redpanda Agentic Data Plane**
2605.29082v1 by Tyler Akidau, Tyler Rockwood, Johannes Brüderl, Marc Millstone

AI agents are increasingly expected to operate as digital employees: accessing enterprise data, making decisions, and taking actions autonomously. But agents are simultaneously less predictable than humans -- prone to hallucination, misinterpretation, and adversarial manipulation -- and more technically capable: with deep system knowledge and high-throughput interfaces cascading damage at machine speed. This combination makes it unsafe to rely on agents to faithfully interpret or propagate security-critical metadata such as access policies, data classifications, and behavioral constraints.
  We present the Redpanda Agentic Data Plane (ADP), an architecture built around out-of-band metadata channels: infrastructure pathways that carry security context, policy signals, and audit trails deterministically, entirely outside the agent's read and write path and across heterogeneous infrastructure. These channels enforce governance at every stage of the agent lifecycle -- scoping data access on the way in, constraining actions during execution, and capturing tamper-proof transcripts on the way out.
  We demonstrate ADP with a multi-agent portfolio rebalancing system in which autonomous agents monitor markets, make trade decisions, and execute orders across isolated client accounts -- with per-client data scoping, trade approval thresholds, and tamper-proof audit trails all enforced by out-of-band channels the agents can neither see nor bypass.

摘要：AI 代理人越來越被期望作為數位員工運作：訪問企業數據、做出決策並自主採取行動。<lb/>但代理人同時比人類更難以預測——容易出現幻覺、誤解和對抗性操控——而且技術能力更強：擁有深厚的系統知識和高吞吐量的介面，以機器速度造成連鎖損害。<lb/>這種組合使得依賴代理人忠實解釋或傳播安全關鍵的元數據（如訪問政策、數據分類和行為約束）變得不安全。<lb/>我們提出了 Redpanda 代理數據平面（ADP），這是一種圍繞帶外元數據通道構建的架構：這些基礎設施通道以確定性方式傳遞安全上下文、政策信號和審計記錄，完全在代理的讀寫路徑之外，並跨越異構基礎設施。<lb/>這些通道在代理生命週期的每個階段強制執行治理——在進入時範圍限制數據訪問，在執行期間約束行動，並在退出時捕獲防篡改的記錄。<lb/>我們用一個多代理組合再平衡系統展示 ADP，其中自主代理監控市場、做出交易決策並在隔離的客戶帳戶中執行訂單——每個客戶的數據範圍、交易批准閾值和防篡改的審計記錄均由代理無法看到或繞過的帶外通道強制執行。

##### **Rethinking Memory as Continuously Evolving Connectivity**
2605.28773v1 by Jizhan Fang, Buqiang Xu, Zhixian Wang, Haoliang Cao, Xinle Deng, Baohua Dong, Hangcheng Zhu, Ruohui Huang, Gang Yu, Ying Wei, Guozhou Zheng, Feiyu Xiong, Haofen Wang, Huajun Chen, Ningyu Zhang

Existing memory-augmented LLM agents often treat memory as a static repository with pre-defined representations and fixed retrieval pipelines, which is brittle in dynamic agentic environments where feedback, task variation, and heterogeneous signals continuously reshape what should be remembered and how it should be connected. To address this, we propose FluxMem, a connectivity-evolving memory framework that models memory as a heterogeneous graph and progressively refines its topology through three stages: initial connection formation, feedback-driven refinement, and long-term consolidation. During execution, FluxMem repairs missing links, prunes interference, aligns abstraction granularity, and distills recurrent successful trajectories into reusable procedural circuits, guided by one metric for memory generalizability and evolutionary maturity. Across three fundamentally distinct benchmarks including LoCoMo, Mind2Web, and GAIA, FluxMem achieves consistent state-of-the-art performance, demonstrating strong adaptation and generalization in complex agentic environments. The code will be open-sourced in https://github.com/zjunlp/LightMem.

摘要：現有的記憶增強 LLM 代理通常將記憶視為一個靜態的資料庫，擁有預定義的表示和固定的檢索管道，這在動態的代理環境中是脆弱的，因為反饋、任務變化和異質信號不斷重塑應該記住的內容及其連結方式。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了 FluxMem，一個連接演變的記憶框架，將記憶建模為一個異質圖，並通過三個階段逐步完善其拓撲：初始連接形成、基於反饋的精煉和長期鞏固。在執行過程中，FluxMem 修復缺失的連結、修剪干擾、對齊抽象粒度，並將重複成功的路徑提煉為可重用的程序電路，這一切都受到一個記憶泛化和演化成熟度的指標指導。在包括 LoCoMo、Mind2Web 和 GAIA 在內的三個根本上不同的基準測試中，FluxMem 實現了一致的最先進性能，展示了在複雜代理環境中的強適應性和泛化能力。代碼將在 https://github.com/zjunlp/LightMem 開源。

##### **CORE: Contrastive Reflection Enables Rapid Improvements in Reasoning**
2605.28742v1 by Linas Nasvytis, Simon Jerome Han, Ben Prystawski, Satchel Grant, Noah D. Goodman, Judith E. Fan

Language models can use verifiable rewards to improve at a wide variety of reasoning tasks. However, both parametric (e.g. RLVR) and non-parametric (e.g. prompt optimization) approaches to doing so typically require hundreds of training samples and thousands of model rollouts, making them expensive in the best case and intractable in the worst. To address this challenge, we introduce Contrastive Reflection (CORE), a non-parametric learning algorithm that compares past reasoning traces to generate insights: short natural-language descriptions of reasoning strategies and constraints that capture differences between successful and unsuccessful problem attempts. Across four reasoning tasks, we demonstrate that CORE enables more rapid improvement than both parametric (GRPO) and non-parametric (GEPA, episodic RAG, and MemRL) methods, while using fewer rollouts. Under fixed rollout budgets with as few as five training samples, we then show that CORE also achieves comparable or greater performance gains than each baseline. Finally, we highlight how CORE is also substantially more context-efficient than non-parametric baselines, requiring fewer prompt tokens while storing learned knowledge as compact, interpretable natural-language insights. Our results therefore suggest that distilling contrasts between successful and unsuccessful reasoning traces into abstract and useful insights can provide a more efficient and interpretable route to model self-improvement than weight updates, prompt optimization, or direct reuse of stored reasoning traces.

摘要：語言模型可以使用可驗證的獎勵來改善各種推理任務。<lb/>然而，無論是參數化（例如 RLVR）還是非參數化（例如提示優化）的方法，通常都需要數百個訓練樣本和數千次模型回合，這使得它們在最佳情況下成本高昂，而在最糟糕的情況下則難以處理。<lb/>為了解決這一挑戰，我們引入了對比反思（CORE），這是一種非參數學習算法，通過比較過去的推理痕跡來生成見解：短小的自然語言描述，闡述推理策略和約束，捕捉成功和不成功的問題嘗試之間的差異。<lb/>在四個推理任務中，我們展示了 CORE 使得改進速度比參數化（GRPO）和非參數化（GEPA、情節 RAG 和 MemRL）方法更快，同時使用更少的回合。<lb/>在固定的回合預算下，即使只有五個訓練樣本，我們也展示了 CORE 能夠實現與每個基線相當或更大的性能增益。<lb/>最後，我們強調 CORE 在上下文效率上也顯著優於非參數基線，需求更少的提示標記，同時將學到的知識以緊湊、可解釋的自然語言見解進行存儲。<lb/>因此，我們的結果表明，將成功和不成功的推理痕跡之間的對比提煉成抽象且有用的見解，可以提供比權重更新、提示優化或直接重用存儲的推理痕跡更有效且可解釋的模型自我改進途徑。

##### **BIRDNet: Mining and Encoding Boolean Implication Knowledge Graphs as Interpretable Deep Neural Networks**
2605.28739v1 by Tirtharaj Dash

Tabular data in knowledge-rich domains often carries a latent prior in the form of Boolean implication relationships (BIRs) between pairs of features. We mine such relationships with a sparse-exception binomial test. The mined implications form a typed directed graph, equivalent to a propositional rule base of 2-literal clauses. We encode this graph as the connectivity of a layered neural network, called BIRDNet, in which each hidden unit corresponds to one mined rule and binds only to its two features. We show two consequences of this design: First, the architecture is sparse by construction: at most $2/d$ of the weights in each BIR layer are active, where $d$ is the input dimension. Second, the model is interpretable: every trained unit keeps a stable symbolic identity, so rules can be read off the network without surrogate models. Unlike most neurosymbolic models, BIRDNet does not consume an external rule base; its structural prior is mined from the data. We evaluate BIRDNet on six transcriptomic and proteomic benchmarks. Our results show that BIRDNet stays within 0.02 AUROC of the strongest dense baseline, at a small accuracy cost, while using up to $96\times$ fewer active parameters than an architecture-matched dense MLP. First-layer rules recover known biological signatures across multiple cancer subtypes and tissue types, including canonical amplicons, lineage-defining co-expression modules, and immune-infiltration markers. Data and code are available at: https://github.com/MAHI-Group/BIRDNet.

摘要：知識豐富領域中的表格數據通常隱含著布林推理關係（BIRs），這些關係存在於特徵對之間。 我們利用稀疏例外的二項檢驗來挖掘這些關係。 挖掘出的推理形成了一個類型化的有向圖，等同於由2個文字子句組成的命題規則庫。 我們將這個圖編碼為一個分層神經網絡的連接性，稱為BIRDNet，其中每個隱藏單元對應於一個挖掘出的規則，並僅與其兩個特徵綁定。 我們展示了這一設計的兩個結果：首先，該架構在結構上是稀疏的：每個BIR層中最多有$2/d$的權重是活躍的，其中$d$是輸入維度。 其次，該模型是可解釋的：每個訓練單元保持穩定的符號身份，因此可以在不使用替代模型的情況下從網絡中讀取規則。 與大多數神經符號模型不同，BIRDNet不消耗外部規則庫；其結構先驗是從數據中挖掘出來的。 我們在六個轉錄組和蛋白質組基準上評估了BIRDNet。 我們的結果顯示，BIRDNet的AUROC值與最強的密集基線相差不超過0.02，雖然準確度略有損失，但使用的活躍參數數量比架構匹配的密集MLP少了多達$96\times$。 第一層規則恢復了多種癌症亞型和組織類型中的已知生物標誌，包括典型的擴增子、血統定義的共表達模塊和免疫滲透標記。 數據和代碼可在以下鏈接獲得：https://github.com/MAHI-Group/BIRDNet。

##### **Code as a Weapon: A Consensus-Labeled Prompt Bank for Measuring Coding-Model Compliance with Malicious-Code Requests**
2605.28734v1 by Richard J. Young, Gregory D. Moody

A general-purpose language model that answers a harmful question returns text; a coding model that complies with a malicious request can return a working weapon -- a keylogger, a ransomware stub, an exploit that runs as written. This asymmetry in the severity of a single act of compliance implies coding-specialized models should clear a higher refusal bar than general-purpose chat models, not a lower one, yet the field cannot presently tell whether they do. Refusal benchmarks for malicious code are fragmented: they mix requests for executable software (ready-to-run weapons) with requests for harmful security knowledge (information a human must still operationalise) and report refusal rates over non-comparable corpora, so no single statistic measures the property that actually matters. This paper introduces an expanded consensus-labeled prompt bank that distinguishes between these two request types and provides a construct-stable substrate for cross-corpus coding-model compliance measurement. Eight corpora (ASTRA, CySecBench, AdvBench/harmful_behaviors, JailbreakBench, MalwareBench, RedCode, RMCBench, Scam2Prompt) are consolidated and classified under a five-judge consensus protocol (6,675 prompts x 5 judges = 33,375 calls). The panel reaches Fleiss' kappa = 0.767 [95% CI 0.755, 0.777] ("substantial"); 95.0% of prompts draw at least four agreeing judges, 76.9% are unanimous, and the panel reproduces the earlier four-corpus release at Cohen's kappa = 0.952 on the 3,133 shared prompts. The released bank comprises 4,748 consensus-CODE prompts (executable malicious code requests) and 1,923 consensus-KNOWLEDGE prompts (harmful security knowledge requests). The bank is the validated instrument the field has lacked: a reliability-quantified basis for testing whether coding models meet the stricter refusal standard their executable output demands.

摘要：一個通用語言模型回答有害問題時會返回文本；一個符合惡意請求的編碼模型則可以返回一個有效的武器——鍵盤記錄器、勒索軟體存根、按照要求運行的漏洞。這種單一遵從行為的嚴重性不對稱意味著專門編碼的模型應該設置比通用聊天模型更高的拒絕門檻，而不是更低的，然而目前該領域無法判斷它們是否如此。對於惡意代碼的拒絕基準是零散的：它們將可執行軟體的請求（隨時可運行的武器）與有害安全知識的請求（人類仍需將其操作化的信息）混合在一起，並在不可比較的語料庫上報告拒絕率，因此沒有單一統計數據能夠衡量實際重要的屬性。本文介紹了一個擴展的共識標記提示庫，區分這兩種類型的請求，並提供了一個結構穩定的基底，用於跨語料庫編碼模型的遵從性測量。八個語料庫（ASTRA、CySecBench、AdvBench/harmful_behaviors、JailbreakBench、MalwareBench、RedCode、RMCBench、Scam2Prompt）被整合並根據五位評審的共識協議進行分類（6,675個提示 x 5位評審 = 33,375次調用）。小組達到Fleiss' kappa = 0.767 [95% CI 0.755, 0.777]（"相當可觀"）；95.0%的提示至少有四位評審一致同意，76.9%是全體一致的，並且小組在3,133個共享提示上重現了早期的四語料庫發布，Cohen's kappa = 0.952。發布的提示庫包含4,748個共識-CODE提示（可執行的惡意代碼請求）和1,923個共識-KNOWLEDGE提示（有害安全知識請求）。該庫是該領域所缺乏的經過驗證的工具：一個可靠性量化的基礎，用於測試編碼模型是否符合其可執行輸出所要求的更嚴格的拒絕標準。

##### **MemTrace: Tracing and Attributing Errors in Large Language Model Memory Systems**
2605.28732v1 by Xinle Deng, Ruobin Zhong, Hujin Peng, Xiaoben Lu, Yanzhe Wu, Guang Li, Buqiang Xu, Yunzhi Yao, Jizhan Fang, Haoliang Cao, Junjie Guo, Yuan Yuan, Ziqing Ma, Yuanqiang Yu, Rui Hu, Baohua Dong, Hangcheng Zhu, Ningyu Zhang

Memory is essential for enabling large language models to support long-horizon reasoning, yet existing memory systems remain unreliable and difficult to debug. Tracing memory's dynamic evolution is crucial to understand how information is synthesized, propagated, or corrupted over time. In this work, we study the new problem of error tracing and attribution in LLM memory systems. We propose a novel framework that transforms memory pipelines into executable memory evolution graphs, enabling fine-grained tracing of operational information flow. We then construct MemTraceBench, a benchmark collected from representative memory systems such as Long-Context, RAG, Mem0, and EverMemOS, to systematically study memory failure modes. We further introduce an automatic attribution method that iteratively traces operation subgraphs to pinpoint the root cause of any failed case. Our analysis reveals that memory failures are systematic, stemming from operation-level issues like information loss and retrieval misalignment. Crucially, we leverage these fine-grained attribution signals to guide downstream prompt optimization, establishing a closed-loop system that automatically corrects faults and boosts end-task performance by up to 7.62%. Code will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/MemTrace.

摘要：記憶對於使大型語言模型支持長期推理至關重要，但現有的記憶系統仍然不可靠且難以調試。追蹤記憶的動態演變對於理解信息如何隨時間合成、傳播或損壞至關重要。在這項工作中，我們研究了LLM記憶系統中錯誤追蹤和歸因的新問題。我們提出了一個新穎的框架，將記憶管道轉換為可執行的記憶演變圖，從而實現操作信息流的細粒度追蹤。然後，我們構建了MemTraceBench，這是一個從代表性記憶系統（如Long-Context、RAG、Mem0和EverMemOS）收集的基準，以系統地研究記憶故障模式。我們進一步引入了一種自動歸因方法，通過迭代追蹤操作子圖來確定任何失敗案例的根本原因。我們的分析顯示，記憶故障是系統性的，源於操作級別的問題，如信息丟失和檢索錯位。關鍵是，我們利用這些細粒度的歸因信號來指導下游提示優化，建立一個閉環系統，自動修正故障，並將最終任務性能提高至7.62%。代碼將在 https://github.com/zjunlp/MemTrace 發佈。

##### **LiveBrowseComp: Are Search Agents Searching, or Just Verifying What They Already Know?**
2605.28721v1 by HuiMing Fan, Xiao Wang, Zheng Chu, Qianyu Wang, Zhuoyao Wang, Ming Liu, Bing Qin,  XingYu

Are LLM-based search agents genuinely searching, or using the web to verify what they already know? We study this question on BrowseComp with three diagnostics. Our analysis reveals Intrinsic Knowledge Dependence (IKD): even with tool access, agents often rely on intrinsic knowledge -- information encoded in the model before retrieval -- rather than on external evidence. Agents answer up to 44.5% of BrowseComp questions without tools, generate more than half of their search queries from internally produced hypotheses rather than retrieved leads, and perform worse than closed-book baselines when answer-supporting evidence is removed. These results suggest that static search benchmarks can reward memory-backed verification rather than evidence-driven discovery, conflating what agents already know with what they can find. We then introduce LiveBrowseComp, a deep-search benchmark designed to evaluate agents beyond intrinsic coverage. It contains 335 human-authored questions whose answers depend on facts published within the 90 days preceding benchmark construction, drawn from six updated sources and filtered to exclude globally salient events. On LiveBrowseComp, all evaluated agents fall below 2% closed-book accuracy, search-augmented scores drop by 25-40 points relative to BrowseComp, and prior model rankings no longer reliably predict performance. LiveBrowseComp is available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/Forival/LiveBrowseComp.

摘要：LLM 基於的搜尋代理是否真的在搜尋，還是僅僅在使用網路來驗證他們已經知道的東西？我們在 BrowseComp 上通過三個診斷來研究這個問題。分析顯示內在知識依賴（IKD）：即使有工具可用，代理通常依賴於內在知識——在檢索之前編碼在模型中的信息——而不是外部證據。代理在不使用工具的情況下回答多達 44.5% 的 BrowseComp 問題，超過一半的搜尋查詢來自內部生成的假設，而非檢索到的線索，並且在移除支持答案的證據後，表現不如封閉書籍基準。這些結果表明，靜態搜尋基準可能會獎勵基於記憶的驗證，而不是基於證據的發現，混淆了代理已經知道的內容與他們能找到的內容。然後，我們介紹了 LiveBrowseComp，一個深度搜尋基準，旨在評估代理超越內在覆蓋範圍。它包含 335 個人類撰寫的問題，其答案依賴於在基準構建前 90 天內發布的事實，這些事實來自六個更新的來源，並過濾以排除全球突出的事件。在 LiveBrowseComp 上，所有評估的代理的封閉書籍準確率均低於 2%，相較於 BrowseComp，搜尋增強分數下降了 25-40 分，而之前的模型排名不再可靠地預測性能。LiveBrowseComp 可在 https://huggingface.co/datasets/Forival/LiveBrowseComp 獲得。

##### **VeriTrip: A Verifiable Benchmark for Travel Planning Agents over Unstructured Web Corpora**
2605.28683v1 by Yuting Xu, Jiayi Tian, Jian Liang, Xin Xiong, Hang Zhang, Mu Xu, Xiao-Yu Zhang

Existing benchmarks have laid the foundation for travel planning agents by establishing API-centric paradigms. However, as the capabilities of Autonomous Agents continue to advance, their evaluation must evolve beyond simple tool execution toward handling the inherent complexities of the open web. Current benchmarks bypass core cognitive hurdles: they fail to account for information noise, ignore multi-source factual contradictions, and overlook the necessity of grounding visual perception into logical planning. We introduce VeriTrip, a verifiable benchmark designed to meet the increasing demands for agent robustness and reliability. VeriTrip shifts the evaluation focus to evidence-grounded reasoning over unstructured multimodal web corpora. It establishes a Multimodal Retrieval Base (MRB) derived from real-world sources, forcing agents to autonomously orchestrate queries across heterogeneous data. A synchronized Verifiable Knowledge Base (VKB) enables a cell-wise verification protocol that precisely quantifies factual reliability, distinguishing systematic reasoning failures from parametric hallucinations. Our evaluations across leading MLLMs reveal a critical \textit{retrieval-reasoning trade-off}: the cognitive load of autonomous retrieval significantly erodes instruction retention. VeriTrip provides the rigorous foundation necessary for the next generation of planning agents capable of operating in unconstrained, multimodal environments.

摘要：現有的基準已為旅行規劃代理奠定了基礎，通過建立以 API 為中心的範式。<lb/>然而，隨著自主代理能力的不斷提升，它們的評估必須超越簡單的工具執行，轉向處理開放網絡固有的複雜性。<lb/>當前的基準忽略了核心的認知障礙：它們未能考慮信息噪聲，忽視多來源事實矛盾，並且忽略了將視覺感知根植於邏輯規劃的必要性。<lb/>我們介紹了 VeriTrip，一個旨在滿足對代理穩健性和可靠性日益增長需求的可驗證基準。<lb/>VeriTrip 將評估重點轉向基於證據的推理，針對非結構化的多模態網絡語料庫。<lb/>它建立了一個源自現實世界的多模態檢索庫 (MRB)，迫使代理在異質數據中自主協調查詢。<lb/>一個同步的可驗證知識庫 (VKB) 使得細胞級驗證協議成為可能，精確量化事實可靠性，區分系統性推理失敗與參數性幻覺。<lb/>我們在領先的 MLLMs 上的評估揭示了一個關鍵的 \textit{檢索-推理權衡}：自主檢索的認知負擔顯著侵蝕指令保留。<lb/>VeriTrip 提供了下一代能夠在不受限制的多模態環境中運作的規劃代理所需的嚴謹基礎。

##### **An LLM-Based Assistance System for Intuitive and Flexible Capability-Based Planning**
2605.28666v1 by Luis Miguel Vieira da Silva, Nicolas König, Felix Gehlhoff

In modern industry, dynamic environments and the complexity of modular and reconfigurable resources require automated planning of process sequences. Capability-based planning approaches address this by automatically generating plans from semantic knowledge models that describe resource functions in a machine-interpretable form. Their practical use, however, remains limited: solver feedback, especially in the case of unsatisfiability, is difficult to interpret, and the knowledge models require adaptation as operational conditions change or requests become infeasible. This paper presents a hybrid assistance system that augments an existing capability-based Satisfiability Modulo Theories (SMT) planning approach with an Large Language Model (LLM)-based layer for natural-language interaction, explanation, and adaptation. Formal planning correctness remains with the symbolic planner, while the LLM layer handles natural-language access and flexible knowledge model adaptation under explicit Human-in-the-Loop (HitL) approval. The system decomposes into four components: Capability Grounding, Symbolic Planning, Result Interpretation, and Planning Adaptation, realized as a routed agentic workflow in which a central router delegates to five specialized agents. The system is evaluated on a modular production system across four scenario types. Of 23 test cases, 9 of 10 knowledge queries and all 4 satisfiable planning cases were handled correctly, 3 of 4 unsatisfiable cases produced concrete repair proposals, and all 5 adaptive planning scenarios resolved into satisfiable plans through iterative, user-approved knowledge model modifications. The findings confirm that combining formal planning with LLM-based assistance substantially improves accessibility and adaptability in industrial automation.

摘要：在現代工業中，動態環境以及模組化和可重構資源的複雜性要求自動化的過程序列規劃。基於能力的規劃方法通過自動生成計劃來解決這個問題，這些計劃來自於描述資源功能的語義知識模型，並以機器可解釋的形式呈現。然而，它們的實際使用仍然有限：解決器的反饋，特別是在不滿足的情況下，難以解釋，而知識模型需要隨著操作條件的變化或請求變得不可行而進行調整。本文提出了一個混合輔助系統，該系統增強了現有的基於能力的滿足性模組理論（SMT）規劃方法，並加入了一個基於大型語言模型（LLM）的層，用於自然語言互動、解釋和調整。形式規劃的正確性仍由符號規劃者維持，而LLM層則處理自然語言訪問和在明確的人類參與（HitL）批准下的靈活知識模型調整。該系統分解為四個組件：能力基礎、符號規劃、結果解釋和規劃調整，實現為一個路由的智能工作流程，其中中央路由器將任務委派給五個專門的代理。該系統在一個模組化生產系統上進行了四種場景類型的評估。在23個測試案例中，10個知識查詢中有9個和所有4個可滿足的規劃案例均正確處理，4個不滿足的案例中有3個產生了具體的修復提案，所有5個自適應規劃場景都通過迭代的、用戶批准的知識模型修改解決為可滿足的計劃。研究結果確認，將正式規劃與基於LLM的輔助結合，顯著提高了工業自動化中的可及性和適應性。

##### **AutoScientists: Self-Organizing Agent Teams for Long-Running Scientific Experimentation**
2605.28655v1 by Shanghua Gao, Ada Fang, Marinka Zitnik

Scientific research proceeds through iterative cycles of hypothesis generation, experiment design, execution, and revision. AI agents can automate parts of this process, but existing approaches typically follow a single research trajectory or coordinate through a central planner with fixed objectives. As a result, they struggle to sustain parallel exploration, adapt as experimental evidence changes, or preserve knowledge of failed directions over long-running experiments. We introduce AutoScientists, a decentralized team of AI agents for long-running computational scientific experimentation. Agents interpret a shared experimental state, self-organize into teams around promising hypotheses, critique proposals before using experimental compute, and share successes and failures to reduce redundant exploration. Under matched experimental budgets, AutoScientists improves over prior AI agents across biomedical machine learning, language-model training optimization, and protein fitness prediction. On BioML-Bench, spanning biomedical imaging, protein engineering, single-cell omics, and drug discovery, AutoScientists achieves a mean leaderboard percentile of 74.4% across 24 tasks, improving over the strongest AI agent by +8.33%. On GPT training optimization, AutoScientists reaches a target validation bits-per-byte 1.9x faster than Autoresearch and continues discovering improvements from a starting champion where the single-agent approach finds none (7 vs. 0 accepted improvements). On ProteinGym fitness prediction, AutoScientists discovers a method for ACE2-Spike binding that improves over the current state-of-the-art model by +12.5% in Spearman correlation. Applied without modification across all 217 ProteinGym assays, the same method improves over the prior state of the art by +6.5% (Spearman correlation).

摘要：科學研究透過假設生成、實驗設計、執行和修訂的迭代循環進行。AI代理可以自動化這一過程的部分，但現有的方法通常遵循單一的研究軌跡或通過具有固定目標的中央規劃者進行協調。因此，它們在維持平行探索、隨著實驗證據變化而適應或在長期實驗中保留失敗方向的知識方面面臨挑戰。我們介紹了AutoScientists，這是一個去中心化的AI代理團隊，專注於長期計算科學實驗。代理解釋共享的實驗狀態，自我組織成圍繞有前景的假設的團隊，在使用實驗計算之前批評提案，並分享成功和失敗以減少冗餘探索。在匹配的實驗預算下，AutoScientists在生物醫學機器學習、語言模型訓練優化和蛋白質適應性預測方面超越了之前的AI代理。在BioML-Bench上，涵蓋生物醫學成像、蛋白質工程、單細胞組學和藥物發現，AutoScientists在24個任務中達到平均排行榜百分位74.4%，比最強的AI代理提高了+8.33%。在GPT訓練優化方面，AutoScientists達到目標驗證位元每字節的速度比Autoresearch快1.9倍，並繼續從一個起始冠軍中發現改進，而單一代理方法沒有找到任何改進（7對0接受的改進）。在ProteinGym適應性預測中，AutoScientists發現了一種ACE2-Spike結合的方法，將目前的最先進模型在Spearman相關性上提高了+12.5%。在不做修改的情況下應用於所有217個ProteinGym測試，該方法在之前的最先進技術上提高了+6.5%（Spearman相關性）。

##### **GraphSteal: Structural Knowledge Stealing from Graph RAG via Traversal Reconstruction**
2605.28645v1 by Jinze Gu, Qinghua Mao, Xi Lin, Jun Wu

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) enhances LLMs by grounding generation in query-relevant external evidence. Beyond unstructured text corpora, Graph RAG integrates knowledge graphs into the retrieval pipeline, enabling LLMs to access entities, relations, and multi-hop dependencies encoded in structured knowledge. However, the same structured knowledge that empowers Graph RAG also creates a new privacy attack surface. We demonstrate that Graph RAG systems can be turned into structural oracles: through adaptive black-box interactions, an adversary can elicit sufficient relational evidence to reconstruct substantial portions of the hidden knowledge graph. We propose a structure-oriented reconstruction framework that recovers targeted graphs from both local and global perspectives. Specifically, Depth-Wise Heuristic Search extracts fine-grained node attributes by recursively expanding entity-centered evidence, while Breadth-Wise Diffusion Search infers graph topology by propagating across relation-induced neighborhoods. Experiments on generic and healthcare scenarios demonstrate that our method can recover over 90\% of the original knowledge graph from representative Graph RAG systems, revealing sensitive entities, relations, and structural dependencies with high fidelity. Existing guradrails provide limited defense against our attack, highlighting the inherent difficulty of safeguarding structural privacy in Graph RAG pipelines.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）通過將生成基於查詢相關的外部證據來增強大型語言模型（LLMs）。除了非結構化文本語料庫外，圖形 RAG 將知識圖譜整合到檢索管道中，使 LLM 能夠訪問編碼在結構化知識中的實體、關係和多跳依賴。然而，賦予圖形 RAG 能力的相同結構化知識也創造了一個新的隱私攻擊面。我們展示了圖形 RAG 系統可以轉變為結構性神諭：通過自適應黑盒交互，對手可以引出足夠的關係證據，以重建隱藏知識圖譜的相當大部分。我們提出了一個結構導向的重建框架，從局部和全局的角度恢復目標圖。具體而言，深度優化啟發式搜索通過遞歸擴展以實體為中心的證據來提取細粒度的節點屬性，而廣度擴散搜索則通過在關係引發的鄰域中傳播來推斷圖拓撲。在通用和醫療場景上的實驗表明，我們的方法可以從代表性的圖形 RAG 系統中恢復超過 90\% 的原始知識圖，並以高保真度揭示敏感的實體、關係和結構依賴。現有的防護措施對我們的攻擊提供了有限的防禦，突顯了在圖形 RAG 管道中保護結構隱私的固有困難。

##### **Blind PRNG Hijacking: An Undetectable Integrity-Preserving Attack Against LLM Watermarking**
2605.28632v1 by Ziyang You, Huilong He, Xiaoke Yang, Xuxing Lu

Cryptographic watermarking is a leading defense for attributing text generated by large language models (LLMs). Existing schemes, including KGW, Unigram, and DipMark, derive their security guarantees from the assumption that the underlying pseudo-random number generator (PRNG) is trustworthy. This work introduces SeedHijack, the first supply-chain attack on LLM watermarking that is simultaneously (i) blind -- requiring no knowledge of the watermark key, detector, or model logits, (ii) integrity-preserving -- amplifying rather than erasing the watermark signal, and (iii) orthogonal to detection -- the attack-induced bias is statistically independent of all content-side detector statistics, ensuring that amplification and evasion coexist without trade-off. Rather than perturbing generated text, SeedHijack replaces the PRNG at the supply-chain layer, biasing green-list selection without altering output tokens or degrading text quality. Across three watermarking schemes and three open-source LLMs, the attack triggers 0/6 state-of-the-art content-side statistical detectors while inflating the watermark z-score up to 2.42x (system-level defenses such as entropy-source attestation remain orthogonal and complementary). A quantum random number generator (QRNG) countermeasure is shown to fully neutralize the attack while preserving benign watermarking utility. These findings establish PRNG integrity as a first-class security requirement for cryptographic content-provenance systems.

摘要：加密水印技術是歸屬於大型語言模型（LLMs）生成文本的主要防禦措施。現有的方案，包括KGW、Unigram和DipMark，基於假設底層的偽隨機數生成器（PRNG）是可信的，來推導其安全性保證。本研究介紹了SeedHijack，這是對LLM水印的首個供應鏈攻擊，並且同時具備以下特點：(i) 盲目性——不需要了解水印密鑰、檢測器或模型邏輯，(ii) 完整性保護——放大而非抹去水印信號，以及(iii) 與檢測正交——攻擊引起的偏差在統計上與所有內容側檢測器統計數據獨立，確保放大和逃避共存而不需妥協。SeedHijack並不是擾動生成的文本，而是在供應鏈層替換PRNG，偏向綠名單選擇，而不改變輸出標記或降低文本質量。在三個水印方案和三個開源LLM中，該攻擊觸發了0/6個最先進的內容側統計檢測器，同時將水印z-score提升至2.42倍（系統級防禦如熵源驗證仍然是正交和互補的）。量子隨機數生成器（QRNG）對策被證明能完全中和該攻擊，同時保留良性水印的效用。這些發現確立了PRNG的完整性作為加密內容來源系統的一級安全要求。

##### **Measuring Form and Function in Language Models**
2605.28616v1 by Héctor Javier Vázquez Martínez, Charles Yang

We introduce quantitative metrics for child language acquisition to evaluate language models. Our focus is on the formal syntactic and functional discourse properties of determiners in English, which young children acquire early and accurately. We propose Contextual Alternative Choice (CAC), a new prompting method which provides targeted tests for both syntactic and discourse knowledge of language. The method enables direct comparison of language models against children, and more importantly, against statistical benchmarks independently established in empirical research. No current model trained on a comparable amount of data simultaneously meet both formal and functional benchmarks like human children, but some very large models do. We present our results as methodological and technical contributions, with specific emphasis on cognitive status of language models.

摘要：我們引入量化指標來評估語言模型的兒童語言習得。我們的重點是英語中限定詞的正式句法和功能性話語特徵，這些特徵是年幼的孩子早期且準確地習得的。我們提出了上下文替代選擇（CAC），這是一種新的提示方法，提供針對語言的句法和話語知識的有針對性的測試。該方法使語言模型能夠與兒童進行直接比較，更重要的是，與在實證研究中獨立建立的統計基準進行比較。目前沒有任何模型在相似數量的數據上訓練，能同時滿足正式和功能基準，像人類兒童一樣，但一些非常大的模型可以做到。我們將結果作為方法論和技術貢獻呈現，特別強調語言模型的認知狀態。

##### **Adaptive Multimodal Agents-Based Framework for Automatic Workflow Execution**
2605.28607v1 by Susanna Cifani, Mario Luca Bernardi, Marta Cimitile

Modern information systems require autonomous agents capable of navigating complex workflows, yet current methodologies often struggle with the transition from structured metadata parsing to general environmental perception. While the integration of MLLMs has enabled agents to interact directly with GUIs, existing approaches typically treat task sequences as discrete, linear episodes. This fragmentation prevents agents from capturing the underlying transition topology, limiting their effectiveness in novel or non-stationary scenarios. To address this, we propose a novel multimodal multi-agent framework that achieves automatic workflow execution through a distinct two-phase pipeline. First, during an offline discovery phase, the architecture adaptively constructs a topological knowledge base from fragmented execution logs. During inference, agents leverage Adaptive Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) over this fixed, pre-established graph, coupled with a closed-loop collaborative verification protocol to dynamically self-correct and navigate. This graph-based approach facilitates superior task decomposition and adaptive navigation performance. We validate our framework in a real-world context, demonstrating its ability to maintain high reliability and semantic awareness even with limited training data.

摘要：現代資訊系統需要能夠自主導航複雜工作流程的代理，但當前的方法論在從結構化元數據解析過渡到一般環境感知時常常面臨困難。雖然MLLM的整合使得代理能夠直接與GUI互動，但現有的方法通常將任務序列視為離散的線性事件。這種碎片化阻礙了代理捕捉潛在的轉換拓撲，限制了它們在新穎或非穩態場景中的有效性。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了一種新穎的多模態多代理框架，通過一個獨特的兩階段管道實現自動工作流程執行。首先，在離線發現階段，該架構自適應地從碎片化的執行日誌中構建拓撲知識庫。在推理過程中，代理利用自適應檢索增強生成（RAG）在這個固定的、預先建立的圖上，並結合閉環協作驗證協議進行動態自我修正和導航。這種基於圖的方法促進了更優越的任務分解和自適應導航性能。我們在現實世界的背景中驗證了我們的框架，展示了其即使在有限的訓練數據下仍能保持高可靠性和語義意識的能力。

##### **Satisfiability Solving with LLMs: A Matched-Pair Evaluation of Reasoning Capability**
2605.28602v1 by Leizhen Zhang, Shuhan Chen, Sheng Chen

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for tasks that implicitly reduce to Boolean satisfiability (SAT), yet their reasoning ability on SAT remains unclear. We present a systematic study of LLMs on 2-SAT and 3-SAT, together with two canonical reductions, Vertex Cover and discrete 3D packing, to probe representation-invariant reasoning. We first evaluate models using conventional metrics, including accuracy, precision, recall, and F1, as well as the SAT phase-transition setting. We find that these metrics can be misleading: many models obtain high scores by over-predicting satisfiable formulas, fail to reproduce the classical easy-hard-easy signature around the 3-SAT threshold, and degrade sharply as the number of variables grows.
  To address this problem, we introduce a paired-formula protocol based on minimally different satisfiable and unsatisfiable instances, together with Accurate Differentiation Rate (ADR), which requires both members of each pair to be classified correctly. ADR separates reasoning-oriented models from heuristic ones and correlates with witness validity. Beyond CNF, we test cross-representation consistency by converting CNF to Vertex Cover and 3-SAT to discrete 3D packing. Model decisions on CNF and on the corresponding graph or packing instances agree for most models on more than 80 percent of instances, suggesting stable decision rules across representations. Overall, our results show that SAT is a conservative probe for LLM reasoning, and that paired evaluation with ADR provides a more faithful and representation-robust assessment than conventional metrics.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地被用於隱式簡化為布爾滿意性（SAT）的任務，但它們在SAT上的推理能力仍然不明確。我們對LLMs在2-SAT和3-SAT上的系統研究，並結合兩個典型的簡化，頂點覆蓋和離散3D打包，以探討表示不變的推理。我們首先使用傳統指標評估模型，包括準確率、精確率、召回率和F1，以及SAT相位轉換設置。我們發現這些指標可能會產生誤導：許多模型通過過度預測可滿意的公式來獲得高分，未能在3-SAT閾值附近重現經典的易-難-易特徵，並且隨著變量數量的增加而急劇下降。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們引入了一種基於最小不同的可滿意和不可滿意實例的配對公式協議，並結合準確區分率（ADR），該率要求每對的兩個成員都必須被正確分類。ADR將以推理為導向的模型與啟發式模型區分開來，並與見證有效性相關聯。除了CNF，我們通過將CNF轉換為頂點覆蓋和3-SAT轉換為離散3D打包來測試跨表示一致性。對於大多數模型，CNF及其相應的圖形或打包實例的模型決策在超過80%的實例中是一致的，這表明跨表示的穩定決策規則。總體而言，我們的結果顯示SAT是一個保守的LLM推理探測工具，並且配對評估與ADR相比傳統指標提供了更真實和表示穩健的評估。

##### **Models That Know How Evaluations Are Designed Score Safer**
2605.28591v1 by Katharina Deckenbach, Haritz Puerto, Jonas Geiping, Sahar Abdelnabi

The validity of AI safety evaluations depends on models behaving consistently across controlled and deployment settings. Prior work has identified test-time contextual cues, such as hypothetical scenarios, as a source of verbalized evaluation awareness and subsequent behavioral shift. In this paper, we investigate a potential explanation of this phenomenon: evaluation meta-knowledge, defined as parametric knowledge about the structural traits that characterize evaluations. Similar to dataset contamination, where benchmark exposure leads to higher performance through memorization, we hypothesize that models trained on texts describing evaluation practices may implicitly learn to recognize and respond to evaluation-like contexts, for instance, through exposure to scientific articles or social media posts about AI benchmarking. To test this, we fine-tune models on synthetic documents describing evaluation traits such as verifiable structures or moral dilemmas. Evaluating this fine-tuned model on six safety benchmarks, we find that it is significantly safer than the base model and control model. This behavioral shift persists even when restricting the analysis to responses lacking explicit verbalization of evaluation awareness. Our results demonstrate that evaluation meta-knowledge may inflate safety benchmark performance, introducing a novel confounder that is independent of explicit memorization or verbalized evaluation awareness, thus, challenging to detect. These findings have important implications for the design and interpretation of AI safety evaluations. Our code and models are available at https://github.com/compass-group-tue/arxiv2026_evaluation_meta_knowledge.

摘要：AI安全評估的有效性取決於模型在受控環境和部署環境中行為的一致性。先前的研究已經確定了測試時的上下文線索，例如假設情境，作為口頭評估意識和隨後行為轉變的來源。在本文中，我們探討了這一現象的一個潛在解釋：評估元知識，定義為關於特徵化評估的結構特徵的參數知識。類似於數據集污染，其中基準曝光通過記憶導致更高的性能，我們假設在描述評估實踐的文本上訓練的模型可能會隱性地學會識別和響應類似評估的上下文，例如，通過接觸有關AI基準的科學文章或社交媒體帖子。為了測試這一點，我們對描述評估特徵的合成文檔進行了微調，例如可驗證的結構或道德困境。在六個安全基準上評估這個微調模型，我們發現它比基礎模型和控制模型安全性顯著更高。即使在限制分析到缺乏明確口頭評估意識的反應時，這種行為轉變仍然持續。我們的結果表明，評估元知識可能會膨脹安全基準的性能，這引入了一個獨立於明確記憶或口頭評估意識的新混淆因子，因此難以檢測。這些發現對AI安全評估的設計和解釋具有重要的啟示。我們的代碼和模型可在 https://github.com/compass-group-tue/arxiv2026_evaluation_meta_knowledge 獲得。

##### **SARAD: LLM-Based Safety-Aware Hybrid Reinforcement Learning with Collision Prediction for Autonomous Driving**
2605.28583v1 by Kangyu Wu, Peng Cui, Guoxi Chen, Ya Zhang

Ensuring both safety and efficiency in decision-making for autonomous driving systems remains a fundamental challenge. Traditional Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) suffers from unsafe random exploration and slow convergence, while Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate inherent latency in real-time inference operations. To address these limitations, this paper proposes SARAD, a novel safety-aware hybrid framework that synergizes LLMs and DRL for autonomous driving. SARAD substitutes the random exploration of DRL with Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG)-enhanced, LLM-guided decisions sourced from a dynamic expert knowledge repository. An attention discriminator is proposed to integrate the prior knowledge of LLMs into DRL policy optimization. A collision predictor module, fine-tuned with historical collision data, is further designed to improve vehicle safety. Extensive experiments show that SARAD achieves significant performance improvements in the Highway-Env simulator, validating the effectiveness of the proposed model in autonomous driving.

摘要：確保自動駕駛系統在決策過程中的安全性和效率仍然是一個基本挑戰。傳統的深度強化學習（DRL）存在不安全的隨機探索和收斂速度慢的問題，而大型語言模型（LLMs）在實時推理操作中顯示出固有的延遲。為了解決這些限制，本文提出了SARAD，一種新穎的安全意識混合框架，將LLMs和DRL協同應用於自動駕駛。SARAD用從動態專家知識庫中獲取的檢索增強生成（RAG）增強的、LLM引導的決策替代了DRL的隨機探索。提出了一個注意力鑑別器，以將LLMs的先驗知識整合到DRL政策優化中。進一步設計了一個碰撞預測模塊，通過歷史碰撞數據進行微調，以提高車輛安全性。大量實驗表明，SARAD在高速公路環境模擬器中實現了顯著的性能提升，驗證了所提出模型在自動駕駛中的有效性。

##### **Cultural Binding Heads in Language Models**
2605.28543v1 by Avrile Floro, Luca Benedetto

LLMs often default to equal treatment across cultural groups, even though context warrants differentiation: this is a lack of difference awareness. Using mechanistic interpretability and a factorial design on the N4 cultural appropriation benchmark from Wang et al. (2025), we identify 2-3 mid-layer attention heads per model that contribute causally to cultural binding across eight models (four architectures, base and instruct). Cultural binding is the process of associating cultural items with the appropriate identity. Knockout of the identity-to-item edges on these heads lowers the binding strength by 9-23%. The identified heads transfer from instruct to base models, suggesting that cultural binding is created at pre-training. An $α$-scaling shows a graded dose-response and moderate amplification steering at generation ($α= 2-3$) increases cultural differentiation accuracy by 1-3 pp while leaving neutral reasoning mostly intact. A knowledge probing task shows that models know 3-5 times more than they act upon it, indicating that the bottleneck lies in routing and not knowledge.

摘要：LLMs 通常在文化群體之間默認平等對待，即使上下文要求區分：這是缺乏差異意識。使用機械可解釋性和基於 Wang et al. (2025) 的 N4 文化挪用基準的因子設計，我們識別出每個模型中有 2-3 個中層注意力頭，這些頭在八個模型（四種架構，基礎和指導）中對文化綁定有因果貢獻。文化綁定是將文化項目與適當身份相關聯的過程。對這些頭的身份到項目邊緣進行剔除會使綁定強度降低 9-23%。識別出的頭從指導模型轉移到基礎模型，這表明文化綁定是在預訓練階段創建的。$α$-縮放顯示出分級劑量反應和中等放大，生成時的引導 ($α= 2-3$) 將文化區分準確性提高 1-3 個百分點，同時保持中立推理基本不變。一項知識探測任務顯示模型知道的內容是其實際行動的 3-5 倍，這表明瓶頸在於路由而不是知識。

##### **GUI-CIDER: Mid-training GUI Agents via Causal Internalization and Density-aware Exemplar Reselection**
2605.28534v1 by Zheng Wu, Chengcheng Han, Zhengxi Lu, Tianjie Ju, Yanyu Chen, Qi Gu, Xunliang Cai, Zhuosheng Zhang

Despite the rapid progress of multimodal large language models in building Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents, their real-world task completion is fundamentally bottlenecked by a lack of world knowledge about GUI operations. Existing solutions typically rely on expensive multi-agent scaffolding or conventional post-training paradigms, such as Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL). However, post-training only allows agents to implicitly absorb world knowledge through action annotations or reward signals, leading to inefficient trajectory memorization rather than genuine comprehension. Therefore, an approach that enables explicit learning of this knowledge is imperative. To this end, we propose GUI-CIDER, a mid-training method that explicitly internalizes GUI world knowledge through Causal Internalization and Density-aware Exemplar Reselection. GUI-CIDER operates in three stages: (1) data synthesis, which distills static planning and dynamic causal knowledge from GUI trajectories into text; (2) exemplar reselection, which filters the corpus by rewarding causal structures and penalizing semantic redundancy; and (3) mid-training, where the refined data is used to embed the acquired knowledge. Extensive experiments on two GUI knowledge benchmarks and three task completion benchmarks demonstrate that GUI-CIDER consistently improves both the agent's understanding of GUI operations and its task success rates.The codes are available at https://github.com/Wuzheng02/GUI-CIDER.

摘要：儘管多模態大型語言模型在構建圖形用戶界面（GUI）代理方面取得了快速進展，但它們在現實世界中完成任務的能力根本上受到對GUI操作缺乏世界知識的瓶頸。現有的解決方案通常依賴於昂貴的多代理搭建或傳統的後訓練範式，如監督微調（SFT）和強化學習（RL）。然而，後訓練僅允許代理通過行動註釋或獎勵信號隱性地吸收世界知識，導致效率低下的軌跡記憶，而非真正的理解。因此，能夠明確學習這些知識的方法是必要的。為此，我們提出了GUI-CIDER，一種中期訓練方法，通過因果內化和密度感知範例重新選擇明確內化GUI世界知識。GUI-CIDER在三個階段運作：（1）數據合成，將靜態規劃和動態因果知識從GUI軌跡提煉成文本；（2）範例重新選擇，通過獎勵因果結構和懲罰語義冗餘來過濾語料庫；（3）中期訓練，使用精煉後的數據來嵌入所獲得的知識。在兩個GUI知識基準和三個任務完成基準上的大量實驗表明，GUI-CIDER始終提高了代理對GUI操作的理解及其任務成功率。代碼可在 https://github.com/Wuzheng02/GUI-CIDER 獲得。

##### **Entropy-aware Masking for Masked Language Modeling**
2605.28526v1 by Gokul Srinivasagan, Kai Hartung, Munir Georges

Masked language modeling has become a standard pretraining objective for training encoder-based language models. In this approach, certain tokens in the input are masked, and the model learns to predict them using the surrounding context. This process enables the model to capture both syntactic and semantic properties of language. Conventionally, the tokens selected for masking are chosen at random, which may not always yield the most effective learning signals. In this work, we examine a token masking strategy based on entropy distribution. We use the model's entropy over token predictions to identify which tokens should be masked. This method aims to target tokens that are more informative and uncertain to improve the training efficacy. We also propose a novel self-masking approach that enhances training efficiency without relying on an external reference model. Experimental results demonstrate that our method achieves an average performance improvement of 5% in GLUE scores compared to the baseline. Further, we experiment with combining knowledge distillation with entropy masking, resulting in the best overall results.

##### **Let Relations Speak: An End-to-End LLM-GNN Soft Prompt Framework for Fraud Detection**

In recent years, Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown great capability in processing graph tasks such as fraud detection. Additionally, fraud detection often exhibits multi-relational complexity, where current methods struggle to capture this deep semantic information. To address these challenges, we propose LLM-GNN Soft Prompt Framework (LGSPF). Specifically, LGSPF bridges the graph structure and semantic space using soft prompt to eliminate reliance on text. ##### **ProvMind: Provenance-grounded reasoning for materials synthesis**
2605.28487v1 by Yiming Zhang, Ryo Tamura, Koji Tsuda

Materials process optimization requires reasoning over routes, conditions, tools and causal dependencies, yet most computational formulations flatten synthesis procedures into text or ordered steps. ##### **From Learning Resources to Competencies: LLM-Based Tagging with Evidence and Graph Constraints**
2605.28483v1 by Ngoc Luyen Le, Marie-Hélène Abel, Bertrand Laforge

Linking learning resources to a structured competency framework is key to enabling competency-based search and curriculum analytics in Learning Management Systems (LMS). However, manual tagging is labor-intensive, and fully automatic methods often lack transparency. In this paper, we present an end-to-end alignment pipeline that uses a large language model (LLM) as a constrained, evidence-producing tagger. LMS resources -both instructional content and assessments -are first segmented into meaningful pedagogical fragments. For each fragment, a small set of candidate competencies is retrieved from structured competency profiles enriched with graph-based context. The LLM then selects the most relevant competencies from this set and provides supporting evidence spans from the fragment text. These predictions are refined using the structure of the competency graph and aggregated at the resource level. We evaluate our approach on a dataset built from the Computer Science department's competency referential at the Université de Technologie de Compiègne (UTC), covering 22 competencies across multiple course materials. Our LLM+BM25+Graph (LBG) pipeline achieves strong results, with a micro-F1 of 0.57 and macro-F1 of 0.50 at the fragment level, 0.51 macro-F1 at the resource level, and an MRR of 0.82outperforming zero-shot and few-shot LLM variants, retrieval/similarity baselines, and supervised classifiers -while also producing more mechanically traceable evidence spans to support human auditing and educational analysis.

摘要：將學習資源與結構化的能力框架聯繫起來是實現基於能力的搜索和課程分析在學習管理系統 (LMS) 中的關鍵。<lb/>然而，手動標記是勞動密集型的，而完全自動化的方法往往缺乏透明度。<lb/>在本文中，我們提出了一個端到端的對齊管道，使用大型語言模型 (LLM) 作為受限的、產生證據的標記器。<lb/>LMS 資源——包括教學內容和評估——首先被分割成有意義的教學片段。<lb/>對於每個片段，從結構化的能力檔案中檢索出一小組候選能力，這些檔案以基於圖的上下文進行豐富。<lb/>然後，LLM 從這組中選擇最相關的能力，並提供來自片段文本的支持證據範圍。<lb/>這些預測使用能力圖的結構進行細化，並在資源層面進行匯總。<lb/>我們在從康皮涅技術大學 (UTC) 的計算機科學系能力參考資料構建的數據集上評估我們的方法，涵蓋了 22 種能力，涉及多個課程材料。<lb/>我們的 LLM+BM25+Graph (LBG) 管道取得了強勁的結果，在片段層面的微 F1 為 0.57，宏 F1 為 0.50，在資源層面的宏 F1 為 0.51，並且 MRR 為 0.82，超越了零樣本和少樣本 LLM 變體、檢索/相似性基準和監督分類器——同時也產生了更多機械可追溯的證據範圍，以支持人類審計和教育分析。

##### **Diffusion Large Language Models for Visual Speech Recognition**
2605.28456v1 by Jeong Hun Yeo, Chae Won Kim, Hyeongseop Rha, Yong Man Ro

Existing Visual Speech Recognition (VSR) systems commonly rely on left-to-right autoregressive decoding, which can force premature decisions on visually ambiguous tokens before sufficient context is available. We propose DLLM-VSR, to the best of our knowledge, the first Diffusion Large Language Model (DLLM)-based VSR framework, formulating transcription as iterative masked denoising with flexible-order decoding. With confidence-based unmasking, DLLM-VSR commits high-confidence positions early and uses the committed tokens as bidirectional context to refine ambiguous ones. To adapt DLLMs to VSR, we introduce a two-stage masked-denoising training strategy that separates visual-to-text content alignment from length modeling. We further observe a performance gap with oracle-length decoding, which assumes access to the true transcript length, indicating that reducing target-length uncertainty can improve DLLM-based VSR. To reduce this gap, we develop length-guided candidate decoding, which uses video duration to construct plausible transcript-length hypotheses, decodes under multiple hypotheses, and reranks candidates using length plausibility and decoding confidence. The proposed method achieves a state-of-the-art WER of 19.5\% on LRS3 using only its labeled training data.

摘要：現有的視覺語音識別（VSR）系統通常依賴從左到右的自回歸解碼，這可能在尚未獲得足夠上下文的情況下，對視覺上模糊的標記做出過早的決策。<lb/>我們提出了DLLM-VSR，據我們所知，這是第一個基於擴散大型語言模型（DLLM）的VSR框架，將轉錄形式化為迭代的遮罩去噪，並採用靈活的順序解碼。<lb/>通過基於信心的去遮罩，DLLM-VSR早期承諾高信心的位置，並將已承諾的標記用作雙向上下文，以精練模糊的標記。<lb/>為了將DLLM適應於VSR，我們引入了一種兩階段的遮罩去噪訓練策略，將視覺到文本的內容對齊與長度建模分開。<lb/>我們進一步觀察到與oracle-length解碼之間存在性能差距，該解碼假設可以獲得真實的轉錄長度，這表明減少目標長度的不確定性可以改善基於DLLM的VSR。<lb/>為了縮小這一差距，我們開發了長度引導的候選解碼，該方法利用視頻持續時間來構建合理的轉錄長度假設，在多個假設下進行解碼，並使用長度合理性和解碼信心對候選進行重新排序。<lb/>所提出的方法在LRS3上僅使用其標記的訓練數據達到了19.5\%的最先進字錯誤率（WER）。

##### **Skill0.5: Joint Skill Internalization and Utilization for Out-of-Distribution Generalization in Agentic Reinforcement Learning**
2605.28424v1 by Jiapeng Zhu, Jianxiang Yu, Yibo Zhao, Chengcheng Han, Qi Gu, Xunliang Cai, Xiang Li, Weining Qian

Equipping large language models with explicit skills has emerged as a promising paradigm for enabling autonomous agents to solve complex tasks. Agent skills can be inherently divided into general skills for broad cognitive transfer and task-specific skills for dynamic execution. However, existing skill-based reinforcement learning (RL) methods typically force a rigid choice between full externalization, which incurs prohibitive context overhead, and full internalization, which risks overfitting and knowledge conflicts. To address this dilemma, we propose Skill0.5, a novel agentic RL framework that explicitly differentiates skill treatments by combining general skill internalization with task-specific skill utilization. Driven by a dynamic, difficulty-aware router, Skill0.5 streams tasks into distinct mastery tiers to apply tailored optimization strategies: it internalizes general skills via privileged distillation to build a cognitive foundation for hard tasks, while using diagnostic probing on easy tasks to penalize shortcuts and enforce specific skill utilization. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop demonstrate that Skill0.5 outperforms both memory-based and skill-based RL baselines, yielding performance improvements across both in-distribution and out-of-distribution scenarios.

摘要：為大型語言模型配備明確的技能已成為使自主代理能夠解決複雜任務的一種有前景的範式。<lb/>代理技能可以本質上分為廣泛認知轉移的通用技能和動態執行的任務特定技能。<lb/>然而，現有的基於技能的強化學習（RL）方法通常迫使在完全外部化（這會產生高昂的上下文開銷）和完全內部化（這會導致過擬合和知識衝突）之間做出僵化的選擇。<lb/>為了解決這一困境，我們提出了Skill0.5，一種新穎的代理RL框架，通過結合通用技能的內部化與任務特定技能的利用，明確區分技能處理。<lb/>Skill0.5由一個動態、難度感知的路由器驅動，將任務流入不同的掌握層級，以應用量身定制的優化策略：它通過特權蒸餾內部化通用技能，以建立解決困難任務的認知基礎，同時對簡單任務進行診斷探測，以懲罰捷徑並強制特定技能的利用。<lb/>在ALFWorld和WebShop上的實驗表明，Skill0.5在性能上超越了基於記憶和基於技能的RL基準，實現在內部分佈和外部分佈場景中的性能提升。

##### **PrionNER: A Named Entity Recognition Dataset for Prion Disease Biomedical Literature**
2605.28375v1 by An Dao, Nhan Ly, Thao Tran, Yuji Matsumoto, Akiko Aizawa

Prion diseases are rare, rapidly progressive, and fatal neurodegenerative disorders that remain difficult to diagnose, particularly in their early stages because of nonspecific clinical presentations. However, to our knowledge, there is no publicly available prion-disease-focused dataset designed to capture a broad range of clinically relevant entities from the biomedical literature. We introduce PrionNER, a manually annotated named entity recognition dataset for prion disease clinical information in PubMed abstracts. The current release comprises 317 abstracts, 2,943 sentences, and 6,955 text-bound entity annotations spanning 15 coarse-grained and 31 fine-grained clinically oriented entity types covering diseases, symptoms, diagnostics, findings, anatomy, treatments, and temporal and statistical evidence. Inter-annotator agreement reaches 81.78 exact-match F1, indicating strong annotation consistency. We benchmark supervised BERT baselines, W2NER, and zero-shot extractors on PrionNER. W2NER is the strongest supervised model, and Gemma-4-31B is the strongest zero-shot model, but the benchmark remains challenging, especially for structurally complex mentions and fine-grained clinically adjacent label distinctions. PrionNER provides a clinically grounded benchmark for prion-disease information extraction and supports research on rare-disease biomedical NLP under low-resource, fine-grained, and non-flat extraction conditions. The dataset, annotation guidelines, and evaluation scripts are available at https://github.com/daotuanan/PrionNER/.

摘要：朊病毒疾病是罕見、快速進展且致命的神經退行性疾病，因為臨床表現不特異，特別是在早期階段，診斷仍然困難。然而，據我們所知，尚無公開可用的專注於朊病毒疾病的數據集，旨在捕捉生物醫學文獻中廣泛的臨床相關實體。我們介紹了PrionNER，一個手動標註的命名實體識別數據集，專注於PubMed摘要中的朊病毒疾病臨床信息。當前版本包含317篇摘要、2,943句子和6,955個文本綁定的實體標註，涵蓋15種粗粒度和31種細粒度的臨床導向實體類型，包括疾病、症狀、診斷、發現、解剖學、治療以及時間和統計證據。標註者之間的一致性達到81.78的精確匹配F1，顯示出強大的標註一致性。我們在PrionNER上基準測試了監督式BERT基準、W2NER和零樣本提取器。W2NER是最強的監督模型，而Gemma-4-31B是最強的零樣本模型，但基準測試仍然具有挑戰性，特別是對於結構複雜的提及和細粒度的臨床相近標籤區分。PrionNER為朊病毒疾病信息提取提供了一個臨床基礎的基準，並支持在低資源、細粒度和非平坦提取條件下對罕見疾病生物醫學自然語言處理的研究。數據集、標註指南和評估腳本可在https://github.com/daotuanan/PrionNER/獲取。

##### **Prompt Codebooks: Discrete Compositional Optimization for Language Model Instruction Refinement**
2605.28360v1 by Jyotirmoy Nath, Neeraj Kumar, Brejesh Lall

Automatic prompt optimization (APO) has driven significant gains in LLM-based agentic workflows. However, existing methods treat each task's prompt as a monolithic, instance-blind string optimized through global edits, producing brittle updates and preventing the reuse of learned sub-behaviors. We propose Prompt Codebooks (PCO), a novel compositional prompt optimization framework that recasts APO as discrete learning over a finite vocabulary of natural-language instincts - atomic, reusable instruction units. PCO organizes prompt-construction knowledge in a discrete codebook and routes each input to a small subset of entries via an LLM-based encoder; a generator composes them into a prompt for the frozen target model; a critic emits a structured verdict that decomposes by attribution into per-variable textual gradients, jointly training the encoder, generator, and codebook under a language-valued min-max objective. The resulting routing is per-instance: different inputs in the same task receive different instinct compositions, a regime structurally inexpressible under instance-blind methods. Across six benchmarks on Qwen3-8B and LLaMA-3.1-8B, PCO improves over zero-shot by up to +30.36 points, surpasses the strongest prior baseline (GEPA) by +3.34 on HotpotQA and +1.11 in aggregate, and reduces deployed prompt length by up to 14.1x versus MIPROv2 and 3.0x versus GEPA using only K=16 instincts.

摘要：自動提示優化（APO）在基於大型語言模型（LLM）的代理工作流程中帶來了顯著的增益。<lb/>然而，現有的方法將每個任務的提示視為一個整體的、實例盲目的字符串，通過全局編輯進行優化，這導致了脆弱的更新並阻止了學習到的子行為的重用。<lb/>我們提出了提示代碼簿（PCO），這是一種新穎的組合提示優化框架，它將APO重新構想為在有限的自然語言本能詞彙上進行離散學習——原子化的、可重用的指令單元。<lb/>PCO在一個離散的代碼簿中組織提示構建知識，並通過基於LLM的編碼器將每個輸入路由到一小部分條目；生成器將它們組合成一個針對凍結目標模型的提示；評論者發出一個結構化的判決，通過歸因分解為每個變量的文本梯度，聯合訓練編碼器、生成器和代碼簿，遵循一個以語言為值的最小-最大目標。<lb/>最終的路由是針對每個實例的：同一任務中的不同輸入接收不同的本能組合，這在實例盲方法下是結構上無法表達的。<lb/>在Qwen3-8B和LLaMA-3.1-8B的六個基準測試中，PCO在零-shot上提高了最多30.36分，超過了最強的先前基準（GEPA）在HotpotQA上提高了3.34分，總體上提高了1.11分，並且在使用僅K=16個本能的情況下，將部署的提示長度減少了最多14.1倍，相較於MIPROv2和3.0倍，相較於GEPA。

##### **From Knowing to Doing: A Memory-Controlled Benchmark for LLM Trading Agents on Stock Markets**
2605.28359v1 by Taojie Zhu, Wentao Zhao, Rui Sun, Beidi Luan, Jiacheng Lu, Sinuo Wang, Jing Li, Daxin Jiang, Yonghong He, Zuo Bai

Evaluating whether large language model (LLM) agents can profit in capital markets is increasingly framed as end-to-end trading: place an agent in a historical market, let it trade, and measure portfolio returns. This setup is vulnerable to two evaluation failures. First, long backtests often overlap with the knowledge cutoffs of frontier LLMs, allowing memorized tickers, dates, prices, and market narratives to substitute for investment reasoning. Second, raw returns are a noisy proxy for stock-selection ability, since positive performance may come from market beta, style exposure, or favorable regimes rather than genuine alpha.
  We introduce KTD-Fin (Knowing-To-Doing Financial Benchmark), an end-to-end stock-market trading benchmark that addresses both issues. KTD-Fin uses a data-side masking protocol to anonymize key identifiers and calendar information consistently across prompts and tools, separating historical market memory from investment decision-making. It also incorporates a Barra-style performance attribution framework that decomposes portfolio returns into market, style, and stock-selection alpha components.
  Across ten frontier LLM agents evaluated on the Chinese CSI300 over a 2024--2026 window, masking substantially changes agent rationales, pushing them towards anonymized factor-based reasoning. Attribution analysis further shows that LLM agents' cumulative returns under leakage-controlled evaluation are largely explained by passive market and style exposure, with limited evidence of persistent stock-selection alpha. These findings suggest that financial LLM benchmarks should evaluate not only whether an agent makes money, but also whether the source of returns reflects transferable investment skill. We release KTD-Fin as a reproducible template for leakage-controlled and attribution-aware evaluation of LLM trading agents.

摘要：評估大型語言模型（LLM）代理是否能在資本市場獲利，越來越多地被框架為端到端交易：將代理放置在歷史市場中，讓其進行交易，並測量投資組合回報。這種設置容易受到兩種評估失敗的影響。首先，長期的回測往往與前沿LLM的知識截止日期重疊，允許記憶中的股票代碼、日期、價格和市場敘事取代投資推理。其次，原始回報是股票選擇能力的噪聲代理，因為正向表現可能來自市場貝塔、風格暴露或有利的市場環境，而非真正的阿爾法。

我們推出了KTD-Fin（從知識到行動的金融基準），這是一個端到端的股票市場交易基準，解決了這兩個問題。KTD-Fin使用數據側遮罩協議，持續地在提示和工具中匿名化關鍵標識符和日曆信息，將歷史市場記憶與投資決策分開。它還納入了一個巴拉風格的績效歸因框架，將投資組合回報分解為市場、風格和股票選擇阿爾法成分。

在對2024年至2026年期間的中國CSI300進行評估的十個前沿LLM代理中，遮罩顯著改變了代理的推理，推動它們朝向匿名化的基於因子的推理。歸因分析進一步顯示，在控制洩漏的評估下，LLM代理的累積回報主要由被動市場和風格暴露解釋，對持久股票選擇阿爾法的證據有限。這些發現表明，金融LLM基準應該評估代理不僅是否賺錢，還要評估回報的來源是否反映可轉移的投資技能。我們發布KTD-Fin，作為一個可重現的模板，用於控制洩漏和意識到歸因的LLM交易代理評估。
